# Skyrim:Skybound Watch Pass

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Pass: Skybound Watch Pass ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [Giant Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SouthSkyboundWatchExterior01, SouthSkyboundWatchExterior02, SouthSkyboundWatchExterior03, SouthSkyboundWatchExterior04, NorthSkyboundWatchExterior01, NorthSkyboundWatchExterior02, NorthSkyboundWatchExterior03, SkyboundPass01 | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") West of [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock") | |

Skybound Watch Pass

**Skybound Watch Pass** is a small [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") and [ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider"). It contains only one zone, *[Skybound Watch Pass](#Skybound_Watch_Pass)*.

Although the interior of the pass is named "Skybound Watch Pass", the map markers are named "South Skybound Watch" and "North Skybound Watch", counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. The southern entrance is displayed on the map as a  [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=South+Skybound+Watch&zoom=14&legacy=true), while the northern entrance is displayed as a  [Nordic dwelling](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=North+Skybound+Watch&zoom=14&legacy=true). The southern entrance is south of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), and the northern entrance is southeast of the town.

## Related Quests

- **[Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell")**: Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.

### Exterior: South Skybound Watch

South Skybound Watch

The path that leads up to the pass from near [Orphan Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan_Rock "Skyrim:Orphan Rock") is guarded by a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother") and three [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"). The tower has a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the very top, a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on top of a broken stone table on the level below, and a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on a shelf to the immediate right of the iron door leading into the interior of the pass.

### Exterior: North Skybound Watch

North Skybound Watch

Three bandits reside in the remains of the guardhouse. As you enter through the arch to their sleeping area there is a partly buried [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") on your left, with a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") lying on a broken sideboard. Opposite the arch you enter through is an iron door, with a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") on the ground beneath it. To the right of the door is a table and two chairs holding a [rabbit haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_Haunch "Skyrim:Rabbit Haunch") and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Next to the table is a small cage and beside this is a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer"), and a bench with a copy of *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")* on top. An empty pot hangs above the campfire in the middle of the room, with two unowned bedrolls beside it. Through the door is a lookout point with a pedestal at the end used for the quest [Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell"), while to the left is a novice-locked chest. Follow the stairs down on the right to find the door leading to the interior section of the pass.

### Skybound Watch Pass

The passage links the lowlands of [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") to the mountainous portion of [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") and is divided into three small sections. On either end of the passage are a number of bandits that are cut off by a giant frostbite spider's lair.

Entering from the south leads down a flight of stairs to a room containing a large amount of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") and several [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), with a stairwell in the middle. Wooden spiral stairs lead down to a passage, where three bandits wait. There is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") on your right, and a bit farther, a burial urn on your left. This portion of passage is slightly flooded and contains a large amount of hanging moss. There is an unlocked chest against the east wall, which is trapped with an apprentice-level [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") that triggers [dart traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to fire from the wall. To avoid damage, either disarm before opening, or just stand to the side until they stop. The passage leads to a door, with a giant frostbite spider on the other side of the door facing toward you.

Entering from the northern entrance you will immediately see a couple of bedrolls and then eight hanging moss growing from the ceiling. If sneaking you will see the first of two bandits sitting at the top of a flight of stairs part way down, with the other just to the right out of sight. Beyond the bandits is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"). At the bottom of the stairs is a campfire in front of a set of shelves holding various [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor"), a pair of random [light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Boots "Skyrim:Light Boots"), two small coin purses, and a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Red Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Red_Mountain "Skyrim:Battle of Red Mountain")*. On a sideboard there is a novice-locked chest and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), with a piece of fur armor on the floor next to it. Through the door you will see webbing and spider egg sacs, one of which is harvestable. Follow the stairs down past another harvestable egg sac and several lootable dessicated corpses and web sacs. At the bottom you will encounter the same giant frostbite spider.

## Notes

- The pass contains 23 samples of hanging moss and 8 samples of jazbay grapes.
- A [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") is 240 feet east-southeast of the North Skybound Watch entrance, on the east side of the valley roughly halfway to Orphan Rock.

# Skyrim:Skyforge

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Forge: Skyforge ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skyforge)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Skyforge "Lore:Skyforge")) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Armorer's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Armorer%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:The Armorer's Challenge")* | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | |
| Location | |
| Behind [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Forges/Anvils](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") | 1 |
| # of [Grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") | 1 |

The Skyforge over Jorrvaskr

The **Skyforge** is an ancient forge in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), capable of forging unique weapons and armor. It is currently tended by the greatest [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") in Skyrim, [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). Its heat is used to forge powerful weapons and light the funeral pyres of fallen Companions. The Skyforge is often linked to the sun, and the secret [Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge") beneath is the metaphorical moon, due to its association with [werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf").

The Skyforge at night

## History

Legend tells that the Skyforge has existed since before the area was inhabited. According to the *[Songs of the Return](/wiki/Lore:Songs_of_the_Return "Lore:Songs of the Return")*, the local elves believed it to be a relic of the gods and consequently gave the area a wide berth. [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor") and his [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"), however, were quick to claim the Skyforge as their own once they discovered it and they built their headquarters, [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), here. After this, others started settling, eventually forming what is now the city of Whiterun. According to [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"), the Gray-Mane family has worked at the Skyforge since they first arrived in Whiterun.

## Walkthrough

The Skyforge has four pieces of iron equipment and a book lying around: an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), and a copy of *[The Armorer's Challenge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Armorer%27s_Challenge "Skyrim:The Armorer's Challenge")*. You can also find a grindstone here. The shield, helmet, weapons, and book are free to take regardless whether you're a member of the Companions or not.

:   -  Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the shield, helmet, weapons, and book as owned until you join the Companions.

## Forging

Working at the Skyforge is like working at any other [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). All items that can be crafted at normal forges can also be crafted at the Skyforge, subject to the same [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") perk restrictions.

However, additional crafting options are added to the Skyforge after completing the quest [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead") at the end of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") questline and talking with [Eorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"). "Nord Hero" weapons show up in a new subsection called "Draugr" and "Ancient Nord" armor shows up in the "Daedric" subsection. These items can only be crafted at the Skyforge, but do not require that any [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") perks be unlocked.

:   -  Version 1.2.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") moves the Ancient Nord armor under the "Steel" category, and makes both weapons and armor require the "Steel Smithing" perk to forge.

Although you cannot craft them, Skyforge Steel weapons are available from Eorlund after joining the Companions in [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor"). Eorlund gives you one free weapon, but others can be purchased from him (along with [wolf armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Armor "Skyrim:Wolf Armor")) and you will find a Skyforge Steel Dagger and Greatsword by progressing in the Companions questline. Skyforge Steel weapons are [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven")-tier in damage, but steel-tier in weight and smithing. You can also find Skyforge Steel weapons and Wolf Armor in the [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Merchant_Chests "Skyrim:Containers") underneath.

### Ancient Nord Armor

Ancient Nord armor is low-quality heavy armor, providing the same amount of protection as [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") armor with slightly less weight. All items can be tempered using 1 [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), and having the [Daedric Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Smithing "Skyrim:Daedric Smithing") perk doubles the quality improvement. It can also be found in some Nordic ruins; in particular, it's commonly available in [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost"). There is no Ancient Nord Shield.

A male [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") wearing ancient Nord armor

A female [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") wearing ancient Nord armor

[†](#note_ancientnordgauntlets)Due to an incorrect keyword being set, these gauntlets do *not* add their base armor value of 10 to unarmed damage. Instead, they add 18, because they are misclassified as Daedric. The correct setting for 10 damage would be Iron. This is a perk-specific keyword that does not interact with smithing).
 With the Unofficial Patch, they add 12, because they are misclassified as Steel for the purposes of the perk.

### Nord Hero Weapons

The Skyforge allows you to convert standard [draugr weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Draugr_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") ("Ancient Nord" weapons) into improved "Nord Hero" weapons after completing the main Companions questline and speaking to Eorlund. This can only be done using standard Ancient Nord weapons, not the improved honed and supple Ancient Nord weapons that appear at higher levels. Daggers, maces, and warhammers are not available without the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") (which adds these missing draugr weapon types). The source weapons can generally be obtained in large quantities in any [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") or other [Draugr Crypt](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Draugr_Crypts "Category:Skyrim-Places-Draugr Crypts").

The resulting weapons are all medium-quality weapons, with damage identical to elven, Nordic, or Skyforge steel weapons. However, they are also the lightest available weapons (tied with iron), making them the best option of the four due to lower stamina costs for melee weapons and faster draw time with the bow. All of the weapons can be tempered using 1 [steel ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot") (see [bug](#Bugs)). Having the [Steel Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Smithing "Skyrim:Steel Smithing") perk doubles the quality improvement. While these weapons can only be made at the Skyforge, they can be improved with any grindstone.

If you've completed the Companions questline and still can't forge Nord Hero weapons, talk to Eorlund. He should mention how "the Skyforge feels more... awake."

They can be created in batches of 24 using an equal number of [Ancient Nord Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Arrow "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Arrow") and 1 [Steel Ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"). The patch alters their damage to 16 instead of 24.

## Related Quests

- **[Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms")**: Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").
- **[Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead")**: Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

## Notes

- The [All Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:All_Forge "Skyrim:All Forge")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") added by the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") can be used to craft items usually restricted to the Skyforge.
- The Skyforge also [appeared](/wiki/Legends:Skyforge) in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, with the addition of the *[Heroes of Skyrim](/wiki/Legends:Heroes_of_Skyrim "Legends:Heroes of Skyrim")* card expansion.
- The Ancient Nord Helmet can be used in the [Bone Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Forge "Skyrim:Bone Forge") from the [Gallows Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall "Skyrim:Gallows Hall") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") to create a [Wrathman](/wiki/Skyrim:Wrathman "Skyrim:Wrathman").
- You can enter the forge interface by activating the shelf where *The Armorer's Challenge* is sitting, even though it is not strictly the forge itself. The weapons and armor lying there are also free to take, regardless if you're in the Companions or not. The use of the forge is also not restricted to use of Companions members only, though you will only be able to craft regular armor and weapons, not Nord Hero (which is only available after finishing the Companions questline).
- During [Kodlak's](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane") funeral during [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead"), you won't be able to use the Skyforge until you finish the quest.
- Unlike regular forges, jumping into this one won't set you on fire, and progress towards your [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill won't improve.
- If you clip through the diagonal wooden walls on the north side of Jorrvaskr and turn around, you can easily make your way to the merchant chest underneath the Skyforge.
- [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") drops his Skyforge Steel Greatsword during [Proving Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proving_Honor "Skyrim:Proving Honor"), leaving it free for you to pick up.
- All members of the [Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Gray-Mane") family carry a piece of Skyforge Steel weaponry.
- All Skyforge Steel weapons except for the dagger can be improved at a grindstone. They also benefit from Steel Smithing perk, doubling the improvements made to them.
  - The [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") Creation makes it possible to upgrade the Skyforge Steel Dagger.
    - Be warned, however, that version 4.2.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") removes the ability to upgrade the dagger. Version 4.3 makes it possible to upgrade the dagger once again.
- Skyforge Steel maces, warhammers, and arrows do not exist.
- If you bring [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") to Whiterun, he will express interest in Skyforge Steel and say *"Cicero wants some Skyforge Steel! Sharp, sharp, for easy stabbing!"*
- After Proving Honor is finished, Eorlund will comment on the Skyforge Steel weapon of your selection. You can choose between five weapon types:

| Weapon Type | Comment |
| --- | --- |
| [Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Sword") | *"A blade! It will be as sharp as [Fralia](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane")'s tongue!"* |
| [Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Dagger") | *"Ah, the sneaky type, eh? I think we can fix you right up."* |
| [Battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Battleaxe") | *"Just like [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor") himself."* |
| [Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Greatsword") | *"Sure you can handle that? Ha! Of course you can."* |
| [War Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel War Axe") | *"Now that's a smart weapon. Light, strong, useful. Crack some skulls for me."* |

-  Version 1.2.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") gives the Skyforge a visual heat blur effect.
  -  Version 1.2.6 added the aformentioned heat blur effect to regular forges.

## Bugs

- The Nord Hero bow cannot be tempered.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Even with the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") add-on installed, it is still not possible to craft Nord Hero arrows.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.3, fixes this bug.
- When playing a female character, the Ancient Nord Helmet has the female appearance outside the inventory. Since the vanilla mannequins are male, the helmet cannot be seen when put on a mannequin.
- Ancient Nord Armor, Boots, Helmet, and Gauntlets were incorrectly flagged as Daedric material when they should be Steel.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, addresses this issue. Tempering Ancient Nord Armor now benefits from Steel Smithing perk.
- The stairs leading up to the Skyforge are incorrectly flagged as being metal instead of stone, producing the wrong material sounds.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Skyrim (place)

## Overview

Skyrim

**Skyrim** is the northernmost province of [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") and the main [worldspace](/wiki/Skyrim:Worldspaces "Skyrim:Worldspaces") in the game of *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")*. It is a cold, mountainous region, and the home of the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord"). The province is divided into nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"): [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), and [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)").

For more information, see the [main lore article](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim").

# Skyrim:Skyrim VR

## Overview

*Skyrim VR* box art

| Game Information | | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Development Information | | | | |
| Developer | [Bethesda Softworks](/wiki/General:Bethesda_Softworks "General:Bethesda Softworks") |
| Game Engine | [Creation Engine](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Creation_Engine "wikipedia:Creation Engine")[[1]](#cite_note-SRTechInfo-1) |
| PlayStation VR Release Date | 17 November 2017 |
| PC Release Date | 3 April 2018 |
| [Concept Art](/wiki/Skyrim:Concept_Art "Skyrim:Concept Art") • [Credits](/wiki/Skyrim:Credits "Skyrim:Credits") | |

***The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim VR*** is a [virtual reality](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_reality "wikipedia:Virtual reality") version of *[Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition")* designed for use with [virtual reality headsets](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_reality_headset "wikipedia:Virtual reality headset"). It initially launched on PlayStation VR on 17 November 2017 and later came to PC via SteamVR on 3 April 2018 with support for Oculus Rift, HTC Vive, and Windows Mixed Reality. Similar to the normal *Special Edition*, *Skyrim VR* includes all three [DLCs](/wiki/Skyrim:DLC "Skyrim:DLC").

## Gameplay Differences

- *Skyrim VR* places you within the 3D environment. Your player character is represented by two disembodied hands (or sometimes two controllers) which are manipulated by the handheld controllers.
  - The PC version allows for third person mode, although this is not available in PSVR.
- The main menu is replaced with an interior [playroom](#Playroom) area where you can test out the VR controls. It is a grassy cave with waterfalls, ruins, dummies, and test objects. You start the game in front of a large *Skyrim* logo on a pedestal.
- If enabled, combat requires you to physically use your hands to swing your [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), [block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), cast a [spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells"), or draw and release your [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"). Equipping a held item will cause it to replace your disembodied hand.
- Movement controls are available for [swimming](/wiki/Skyrim:Movement "Skyrim:Movement") and [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak").
- Most [mods](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Mods "Skyrim Mod:Mods") and save games from the *Special Edition* are compatible with *Skyrim VR*. [SKSE](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:SKSE "Skyrim Mod:SKSE")-dlls are a possible exception.
  - The [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creations "Skyrim:Creations") browser and [Verified Creations](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Verified_Creations "Skyrim Mod:Verified Creations") are not available in *Skyrim VR*.
- There are two new Settings menus, VR and VR Performance:
  - VR settings: Turning Mode, Snap Transition, Angle Snap Amount, Rotation Speed, Movement Mode, Compass Position, Main Hand, Height, Movement Speed, Crosshair, Physical Sneaking, Realistic Swimming, Realistic Shield Grip, Realistic Bow Aiming, FOV Filter While Turning, FOV Filter While Moving
  - VR Performance settings: Quality Preset, Supersampling, Dynamic Resolution, Shadow Quality, Shadow Distance, Rain Occlusion, Temporal AA, Foliage Shadows, Disable Model LODS, Disable Tree LODs, Tree LOD Distance, Skinned Trees, Animated Trees, Actor Fade, Item Fade, Object Fade, Grass Fade
- [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") content is not available in *Skyrim VR*.
- [Achievements and trophies](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") are tracked separately for *Skyrim VR* and do not carry over from the original game or from the *Special Edition*.
  - Similar to the *Special Edition*, achievements are disabled when *Skyrim VR* is loaded with mods. However, the use of [console commands](/wiki/Skyrim:Console_Commands "Skyrim:Console Commands") does not disable them.
- The [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") cannot be accessed from within the game using the headset and touch controllers; the keyboard's tilda key must be pressed.
- Similar to the *Special Edition*, *Skyrim VR* does not have [Steam trading card](/wiki/Skyrim:Trading_Cards "Skyrim:Trading Cards") support. The "Cozy Cottage" *Skyrim VR* items are not available in-game and were released as part of the Steam Winter Sale 2018 event.
- The boat ride scene when arriving on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") for the first time is not included in *Skyrim VR*.

## Playroom

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Playroom | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| VRCtest | |

The Main Menu in the Playroom

The **Playroom** is the main menu for *Skyrim VR*. It is a playable space that you can explore, complete with an archery range to practice the new ranged combat. To return to the main menu, simply return to the large *Skyrim* logo in the center of the playroom.

When first launching *Skyrim VR*, you will be walked through a tutorial to help set up your VR controller and comfort options. You spawn at the bottom of the small cave, in front of some Dwemer ruins. You are given the option to choose your dominant hand. This determines many things like what sticks control your movement, and what hands your weapons are placed in. By default, teleportation movement is enabled. You are tasked with teleporting over to the Steed Stone in front of you. Once you reach the stone, you can choose between teleportation or direct movement. Your next objective is to cross a small bridge next to a waterfall to reach the Thief Stone. Once there, you can choose your preferred turning style between snap turning and smooth turning. From here, you are free to make your way to the main area in the center of the cave. Heading directly to the *Skyrim* logo on the pedestal in the middle of the room will bring up the main menu where you can start your game. Alternatively, you are free to be distracted by the archery range on your right, next to some Nordic ruins. On a table, you will find a bow with infinite arrows and an archery range with three target dummies at various distances. Picking up the bow triggers a message box that teaches you how to use the bow in VR. It is recommended to practice your aim if you are new to virtual reality.

|  |
| --- |
| - Your character in the playroom uses the [default player model](/wiki/Skyrim:Prisoner "Skyrim:Prisoner"), a male Nord. - The playroom can be disabled by adding `bLoadVRPlayroom=0` under [VR] in SkyrimVR.ini. This may be required if using certain third party mods that run startup scripts. - The playroom is also used by the game to calculate the player's height. Disabling the playroom also disables physical sneaking. |

# Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Skytemple Ruins

**Skytemple Ruins** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") north of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") containing a [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton").

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.

## Walkthrough

The sparse ruins are at the top of a large glacial mound on an island off the north coast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). They are guarded outside by two archer skeletons and three melee skeletons. To the west is an altar overlooking the sea holding a dead skeleton and a leveled [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Poisons "Skyrim:Potions").

To the east through a novice-locked wooden door is a small burial chamber containing an apprentice-locked boss-level chest guarded by a leveled draugr slumbering in an upright sarcophagus opposite the door. Next to the chest are a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")*, a leveled [regeneration potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and a leveled [lasting potency potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency").

# Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn

## Overview

The Sleeping Giant Inn

The **Sleeping Giant Inn** is a small [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") and tavern in the town of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). It is the first building on the left-hand side coming from Whiterun.

[Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar") is the innkeeper, selling food as well as several alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), which can be used at the [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") in the corner by the door. Rooms are normally rented from [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine"). However, when Delphine is traveling elsewhere, Orgnar will rent you a room, even though his dialogue still tells you to talk to Delphine.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") (Owner) [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") \*  [Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Embry](/wiki/Skyrim:Embry "Skyrim:Embry")  [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") or [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof") † |

\* Leaves once [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") is begun. Orgnar becomes innkeeper and owner.
† They only appear if they were followed during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound").

### Main Quests

- **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
- **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
- **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple").

### Radiant Quests

- **[Alchemy Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Tutorial "Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of potion making.

### Exterior

Wooden steps lead up to a covered porch at the front of the inn with several [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), with several barrels of food around the building. You will often be able to find [Stump](/wiki/Skyrim:Stump "Skyrim:Stump") the [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") on the deck and the children living in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") playing around the inn. At the rear is a small vegetable patch consisting of six [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants, six [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and eight [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") growing, with a further four cabbages in a cart beside it.

| Crops | Plants |
| --- | --- |
| 8 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  6 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  6 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 3 [Thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") |

### Sleeping Giant Inn

Sven performs before an audience

It is a typical Nord inn, with a fire pit down the middle of the common room. The L-shaped counter is at the northeast end, with five long wooden tables along the northwest and southeast walls. There are three doorways leading to bedrooms, two on the northwest side and a larger one on the southeast side. Against the northeast wall is a large vat, several food barrels, a pile of firewood and a set of shelves that hold three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and five bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), with racks hanging from the ceiling in front of them. These hold ten [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), also hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). On the counter are several pieces of cheese, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine. Under the counter and on the floor beside it is a copy of *[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), five more bottles of alto wine and three more bottles of wine.

To the left of the doorway into the larger bedroom is a set of shelves holding several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, while to the right is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") built into a table. The long wooden tables against the walls typically hold bread and a selection of wine and alto wine. However, the table in the western corner of the room also holds a selection of cheeses and two salmon steaks.

The two smaller bedrooms are opposite the larger bedroom. The left-hand bedroom is the room you will be shown to if renting a room for the night and contains a single owned bed in the western corner with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and wardrobe at the foot of the bed and a small round wooden table and chair beside the bed. On top of the wardrobe is a copy of *[The Great War](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Great_War "Skyrim:The Great War")*. On the table is a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). The right-hand bedroom contains a single owned bed in the eastern corner, with an unlocked chest and dresser at the foot of the bed and a small round wooden table and chair beside it. Both of these chests contain only minor loot.

The larger bedroom is [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine")'s room. It contains a single owned bed coming out from the southeast wall, opposite the door with small bedside tables on either side and a narrow table farther to the right with a small coin purse, five bottles of alto wine, and a copy of *[Fall from Glory](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_from_Glory "Skyrim:Fall from Glory")* on top. Against the southwest wall is a wardrobe and a long wooden table and chair. On the table are four bottles of wine, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), several [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a couple loaves of bread, a medium coin purse, and four loose septims.

Delphine's secret room

The wardrobe has a false back panel that opens to reveal a flight of stairs leading down to a secret room containing a central table with a [map of dragon burials](/wiki/Skyrim:Map_of_Dragon_Burials "Skyrim:Map of Dragon Burials") taken from the [dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone") you recovered for [Farengar Secret-Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Farengar_Secret-Fire "Skyrim:Farengar Secret-Fire") from [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") and a copy of *[The Book of the Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_the_Dragonborn "Skyrim:The Book of the Dragonborn")* on top. (The room is revealed to you during the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")). In the western corner is an alchemy lab with a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina") and a [potion of the defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Potion of the Defender") on top and a set of shelves to the left. These hold two [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), five [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), two bunches of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a [potion of destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Destruction "Skyrim:Potion of Destruction"), a [potion of the warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Warrior "Skyrim:Potion of the Warrior"), a potion of stamina, a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health") and a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"). To the left of the shelves is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), with a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), and a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe") on top.

Against the northwest wall are six weapon racks holding a [Blades sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades_Sword "Skyrim:Blades Sword") and several [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons"). Underneath is a quiver of [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") and an unlocked chest. There is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") against the northeast wall, while in the eastern corner is a low table and chair with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a copy of *[The Rise and Fall of the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Blades "Skyrim:The Rise and Fall of the Blades")*, a large coin purse, and four loose septims on the table. There are food sacks to the right, and an unlocked chest farther to the right. Finally, in the southern corner is a practice dummy in front of a couple straw bales.

Delphine uses the inn as a small safehouse and base of operations until the quest [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall"), at which point she gives the inn to [Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar").

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 3 | [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") |  |
| ~5 | Common [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") | Max 6 (6@75%) |
| 1 | Common [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") |  |
| 4 | [Honningbrew Meads](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |  |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |  |
| 10 | Random inn [Food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |  |
| ~1 | Poison [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| ~2 | Rare Ingredients | Max 2 (2@75%) |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |  |
| ~3 | Uncommon Ingredients | Max 4 (4@75%) |
| 3 | [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") |  |

## Notes

- [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven"), unlike most [Bards](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard "Skyrim:Bard") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") does not live at the inn, preferring to live with his mother at the other end of town.
- All barrels can be searched freely once either [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") or [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur") are spoken to during [Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm").
- All low-value and medium-value items in the Inn can be freely taken after stage 10 of the quest [A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark") has been completed. This includes the items in Delphine's secret basement room.
- Several [containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers "Skyrim:Containers") in Sleeping Giant Inn are [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Containers "Skyrim:Containers") for long-term storage, in particular, several containers in Delphine's secret basement room that become available once A Blade in the Dark has been completed. All of the containers in the basement room *except* the barrel are safe for storage—namely two chests and three sacks. Therefore, the chest where your equipment is placed during [Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity") is safe.
- The bed in the right guest room is no longer owned after completing stage 10 of A Blade in the Dark.
- Even if Delphine gives up ownership to [Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar"), her bed cannot be slept on.
- Some items placed inside the barrel next to the door to Delphine's room will be marked as owned, but will not be considered stolen if removed from the barrel.
- There is a failsafe built into the game, where, if your current character location cannot be loaded, your character will instead spawn in front of the bar in the Sleeping Giant Inn.

Sleeping Tree Camp

**Sleeping Tree Camp** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It contains only one zone, *[Sleeping Tree Cave](#Sleeping_Tree_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave_(quest) "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave (quest)")**: Question [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") about an interesting [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message") you found on a [dead Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The camp is almost due west of the [Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower"). The [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") inhabiting the camp will attack those who ignore their warnings to leave. The [Sleeping Tree](/wiki/Lore:Sleeping_Tree "Lore:Sleeping Tree") grows from a pool in the center of the camp along with two [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plants. The tree emits a purplish glow, and its [sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Sap "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Sap") increases health for a limited time with temporary side effects of slowed movement and blurred vision. You can use a sap spigot on the tree to harvest a sample of Sleeping Tree Sap every three in-game days.

### Sleeping Tree Cave

The entrance to the cave is northwest of the tree. The cave is occupied by a single giant that seems to have killed an Orc named [Ulag](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag"). A dose of Sleeping Tree sap and [Ysolda's message](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message") can be found on his body. Next to Ulag's body is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing [leveled loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Three [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") are atop a ledge to the right of the chest, and an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") is along the south wall next to a [mammoth cheese bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl").

Reading Ysolda's message activates a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave_(quest) "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave (quest)") in which [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") will offer money for Sleeping Tree sap. During the quest, Ysolda will tell you two possible origin stories of the tree if asked: that the tree is a piece of the [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") which broke off when the volcano [erupted](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era#4E_5 "Lore:Fourth Era"), or that it was a spore that fell off a flying island. The latter story is likely a [reference](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scrolls_Historical_References#The_Infernal_City_and_Lord_of_Souls "Skyrim:Elder Scrolls Historical References") to the book *[The Infernal City](/wiki/Lore:The_Infernal_City "Lore:The Infernal City")*.

## Notes

- Just southeast of the camp is an unmarked circle of stones containing [a puzzle](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Symbol "Skyrim:Spinning Symbol") and treasure. The puzzle is a standard stone-matching puzzle, with a handle in the middle of the circle next to a stone archway. The stone to the east should be turned to show a snake toward the handle, the stone to the west should show a whale, and the stone to the north should show an eagle. Pull the handle to open a pit in the ground and get the treasure, which includes a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Hypothetical Treachery](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Hypothetical_Treachery "Skyrim:A Hypothetical Treachery")* in a chest.
- Opposite the above circle of stones on a small hill east of the camp are some Nordic ruins with an altar in the center. Lying on this altar is a deceased conjurer, some alchemy ingredients, and a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Liminal Bridges](/wiki/Skyrim:Liminal_Bridges "Skyrim:Liminal Bridges")*. On the northeast side of the altar, hidden under vegetation, is another dead conjurer. Two hostile [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") inhabit the ruins. To the northeast is a unique third skeleton wearing a [black mage hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Hood "Skyrim:Black Mage Hood") standing by three mysterious graves.
- Near the camp to the north is a mammoth skeleton with a human skeleton inside.

## Bugs

- The Sleeping Tree sap spigot can become detached from the tree and fall off. This isn't a problem, as it still gives you the sap even when it's no longer attached to the tree. More problematically, the spigot can also float off and become hard to locate. Area effect spells such as Fireball will affect the spigot, so if it comes off the tree, refrain from using such spells near the pond. You can drag the spigot like any other world item, so if you prefer to keep it safe and don't mind walking, you can take the spigot to a safe place near a fast travel point.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.
  -  You can use the [console command](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") `prid 000AED8B` followed by `moveto player` to teleport the spigot to you if it gets lost. For the best results, stand on even ground. The spigot might otherwise appear inside the terrain where you cannot access it.

# Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Dreamshadow](/wiki/User:Dreamshadow "User:Dreamshadow"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Bwross](/wiki/User:Bwross "User:Bwross"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Question [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") about an interesting [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message") you found on a [dead Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Upon reading [Ysolda's Message](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message") found on [Ulag's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag") corpse |
| Location(s): | [Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave"), [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") will purchase [Sleeping Tree Sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Sap "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Sap") |
| ID: | dunSleepingTreeCampQST |
| Suggested Level: | 1 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

The Sleeping Tree

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Investigate [Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave").
2. Search [Ulag's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag") corpse for [Ysolda's Message](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message").
3. Speak to [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Travel to [Sleeping Tree Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Camp "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Camp") and find the cave inside the camp, northwest of the [Sleeping Tree](/wiki/Lore:Sleeping_Tree "Lore:Sleeping Tree"). Enter the cave and start your investigation. It would be a wise choice to leave the [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and their herd [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") in peace, especially if you are low level. Move swiftly and enter the cave before they turn hostile to you.

[Ulag's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag") corpse can be found on a stone inside the cave with a giant wandering nearby. Search his body, where you'll find Ysolda's Message and a sample of [Sleeping Tree Sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Sap "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Sap"). If you don't want to fight the giant, get out of the cave with the message as quickly as possible. After reading the message, you'll get an idea about what caused Ulag's death. There was an arrangement between Ysolda and Ulag for purchase of the sap, which Ulag would obtain from the Sleeping Tree. Unfortunately, he risked the wrath of the giants one too many times, and ended up paying with his life.

Travel to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and speak to Ysolda about the note you found. Ysolda will quickly realize what happened and offer you the same arrangement she had with Ulag, 150 gold for each sample of sap you bring to her. She'll be satisfied with the deal and remind you *"Be sure to bring any more Sleeping Tree Sap you find to me."* You may also ask her for more information about the Sleeping Tree itself.

## Notes

- [The Official Skyrim Patch 1.5](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.5 "Skyrim:Patch") makes Ysolda essential (to alleviate issues with the [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember") quest, though it also prevents you from accidentally failing this quest as well).

## Quest Stages

| Sleeping Tree Cave (dunSleepingTreeCampQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | *Objective 0:* Speak to Ysolda about Sleeping Tree Sap |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 2, 3, 4, 5, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunSleepingTreeCampQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunSleepingTreeCampQST`.

# Skyrim:Smelter Overseer's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| [Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") | [Loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Loot") Loot |

The entrance to Smelter Overseer's House

**Smelter Overseer's House** is a small home in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), that is home to [Mulush gro-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Mulush_gro-Shugurz "Skyrim:Mulush gro-Shugurz"), the Smelter Overseer, and [Urzoga gra-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Urzoga_gra-Shugurz "Skyrim:Urzoga gra-Shugurz").

The Overseer's House is tucked away behind a rocky outcropping. Initially, it can be very easy to overlook the stairs leading up to it while standing in the smelting area.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Mulush gro-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Mulush_gro-Shugurz "Skyrim:Mulush gro-Shugurz")  [Urzoga gra-Shugurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Urzoga_gra-Shugurz "Skyrim:Urzoga gra-Shugurz")\* |

\* This person works and sleeps in [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine").

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Smelter Overseer's House

There is a small [vegetable](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Vegetables "Skyrim:Food") garden to the east of the [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") outside consisting of two [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") plants and three [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants, with a basket containing two potatoes in front of it. The entrance is normally novice-locked. It is a single story Dwemer style dwelling built into the side of the hill. There are stone shelves on either side of you as soon as you enter. On the shelf on the right is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), barrel containing mead and a crate with a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") on top. While on the shelf to the left is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel, two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a cabbage, a potato and a basket containing a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two more potatoes and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), with an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and bucket containing two pieces of silver ore to the right of the shelf. Coming out from the east wall is a long stone table with a stone chair on either side and two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a bottle of alto wine, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"), a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe") and a [sluice gate key](/wiki/Skyrim:Sluice_Gate_Key "Skyrim:Sluice Gate Key") on top of the table.

Opposite this is a fireplace on the west wall with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging in front and a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a cast iron pot containing a cabbage and [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), and a kettle containing a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a cabbage and three potatoes all on the hearth. To the right of the fireplace is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") on a wooden block and a food barrel with a couple of pieces of cheese on it. Hanging from the ceiling above is a rack holding a rabbit, [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). To the left of the fireplace is a pile of firewood with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against the firewood.

To the south the room narrows, with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on a crate with a food sack beside it, to the east, before a round wooden table and chair with a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast") on top, with an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") stuck into a bale of straw opposite, against the west wall and a pickaxe on the floor nearby. Further south it becomes a corridor to a junction with a door to a bedroom to the west and alcoves to the east and up a couple of stairs to the south. On the east wall, just before the junction is a set of shelves holding a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a cabbage and a few food sacks. In the alcove to the east is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. Between the door to the bedroom and the alcove to the south is a round wooden table holding a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a sample of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales") and a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"). There is a set of shelves against the rear wall in the alcove to the south holding two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a gourd, a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and several pieces of cheese, with another food barrel and sacks to the left.

Through the door is a bedroom consisting of a single owned bed in the southwestern corner with a ledge along the south wall holding a wolf pelt, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a leather strip and a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"). Opposite the door against the west wall is a small square wooden table with a bottle of wine and a bottle of Nord mead on top. To the left of this is a crate with a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") in a wooden bowl on top. with an unlocked wooden chest against the east wall with two silver ingots on the floor beside it.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the left of the entrance door.

## Bugs

- The Sluice Gate Key here doesn't open anything.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. The key has been disabled and removed.

# Skyrim:Smith 'N Slash

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Defeat an [Orc blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and her bandits to obtain an enchanted set of armor.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Added by asking an innkeeper for work after purchasing the [Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)"), [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") |
| Reward: | Set of [enchanted Orcish Plate armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate_Items#Orcish_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate Items") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE054\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate") |

Smith 'N Slash

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Go to the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") [Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)") and read the [dossier](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Dossier:_Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Guard's Dossier: Yakhtu gra-Orkulg").
2. Enter [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine").
3. Kill [Yakhtu gra-Orkulg](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") and obtain [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Yakhtu's Journal") from her body.
4. Read the journal.
5. Kill the bandit chief and retrieve the Orcish Plate armor.

### Guard Barracks

To start this quest go to the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") [Guard Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)") and read the [dossier](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Dossier:_Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Guard's Dossier: Yakhtu gra-Orkulg") which is found on a shelf in the back room.

### Embershard Mine

Head to [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") just southwest of Riverwood. Battle on through the numerous bandits (some noticeably wearing the armor) and make it to the final grand waterfall chamber. Here battle some more bandits including a Chief Bandit wearing the full set and the Orc woman [Yakhtu gra-Orkulg](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu_gra-Orkulg "Skyrim:Yakhtu gra-Orkulg"). Loot her body to find [Yakhtu's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Yakhtu%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Yakhtu's Journal"). Read it to complete the quest.

Finally loot the Bandit Chief to acquire an enchanted full set. Upon leaving the mine you'll have several sets of Orcish Plate Armor including the enchanted one.

## Notes

1. As detailed on the [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") page, the actual chief bandit in here is not actually designated a "Bandit Chief" by name, and appears to just a normal "Bandit", until you search his corpse and find out that he's carrying the good stuff.
2. If the cave is already in a "Cleared" state when you enter it, and has not respawned normally, a few bandits including the chief will still be spawned. The chief will still drop his full enchanted set, but there is no guarantee of getting a full unenchanted set of Orcish Plate from the few bandits in the cave if it has not had time for a full respawn.
3. As a result of the cave having a maximum level as well as a minimum, Yakhtu (min level 15, scales up with player) will be considerably tougher than the bandit chief she technically serves (max level 10).
4. Yakhtu has a named key, which opens a locked chest of smithing supplies next to the table in the large room.

## Quest Stages

| Smith 'N Slash (ccBGSSSE054\_Quest) | | |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE054_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE054_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Smooth Jazbay

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Collect 20 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") for [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi") |
| Location(s): | [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm"), [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") |
| Reward: | Random Potions |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi")) |
| ID: | FreeformSarethiFarm |
| Suggested Level: | Any |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

Avrusa Sarethi in her nirnroot field

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi").
2. Collect 20 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes").
3. Return to Avrusa Sarethi.

## Detailed Walkthrough

[Avrusa Sarethi](/wiki/Skyrim:Avrusa_Sarethi "Skyrim:Avrusa Sarethi") needs a large amount of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") in order to cultivate [nirnroots](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"). She's running low and unable to search out the ingredient herself, as she is preoccupied with her energetic sister and farm chores. She asks you to hunt down twenty grapes for her current nirnroot crop. As Avrusa notes, jazbay grapes are somewhat hard to come by. The plants are indigenous to the volcanic tundra region of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), and while desolate, the tundra is fairly easy to traverse with a few lesser [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and non-hostile [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant").

There are a few locations where it can be found in greater quantities than usual. Along with the quantities available, they are:

- 49 around [Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 47 around [Witchmist Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchmist_Grove "Skyrim:Witchmist Grove") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 35 around [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 33 around [the Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 31 around [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 26 around [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch")), especially along the road heading southeast
- 25 around [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 24 around [Broken Limb Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Limb_Camp "Skyrim:Broken Limb Camp") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 23 around [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))
- 22 around [Riverside Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverside_Shack "Skyrim:Riverside Shack") ([Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"))

Once you have collected twenty samples, head back to Avrusa who will thank you for your aid and reward you with five random potions. You can return to [Sarethi Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Sarethi_Farm "Skyrim:Sarethi Farm") periodically to harvest [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") and [Crimson Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot").

## Bugs

- This quest may leave behind the objective to collect the jazbay grapes due to calling the objective completion before the final item swap is done.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformSarethiFarm stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformSarethiFarm`.

## Overview
