Snapleg Cave

**Snapleg Cave** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower") occupied by [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") and [monsters](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters "Skyrim:Monsters"). It has one interior zone: *[Snapleg Cave](#Snapleg_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") a few paces downhill to the north of the entrance, as well as several patches of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), a [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") fungus growing from a rotten tree trunk, and a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") all near the entrance. The entrance is marked with sharpened stakes and other symbols typical of [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").

### Snapleg Cave

Snapleg Cave hag

The entrance leads into a short tunnel descending to the south and opening into a sinkhole marked with the heads of two [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") on stakes. An earthen ramp descends to the right. At the bottom there are three live skeevers feasting on a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer"). The passage onward is to the south, and is eerily lined with taproot talismans hanging on the walls. Ahead the tunnel turns to the east before opening into a chamber with a grisly elk head mounted on mammoth tusks. This display marks a small encampment with two tents, both occupied by [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"). A skeever, [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), or [troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") will also be wandering around the camp.

A [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") is simmering on a stand beside a fire in front of the first tent. Inside, a table has a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), and a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"). Under the table is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the left of the first tent is a rock formation, on top of which is an open crate hidden behind some foliage; the crate contains a [Staff of Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Paralysis "Skyrim:Staff of Paralysis"), four [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), a [deathbell flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), and a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"). The second tent is to the east of the first, but only displays more trophy heads.

The exit is to the south. A random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") is on the ground just to the left of the mouth of the tunnel. The tunnel twists and turns a fair amount, until a mass of light cobwebs in front holds a desiccated corpse. At this point the tunnel turns to the right, by a patch of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus, more of which is found near the end of the tunnel and in the next chamber. There is another skeever, frostbite spider, or troll in this chamber. The remains of a [mammoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") are on the ground, with a mammoth skull lodged in a hole in the ceiling with [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from it. A [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that fires [ice spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike") is to the east, next to the exit tunnel. Remove the [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") from the pedestal to disarm the trap. To the north is a gap between rocks in the wall, through which you can see a chamber containing a chest, [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and some barrels; this is the final chamber from which is a shortcut back to the entrance.

The next tunnel has a profusion of light cobwebs and opens into a relatively large cavern infested with frostbite spiders and numerous [egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac"), two of which can be harvested. A tunnel heads north from this cavern, while to the east, at the rear of the cavern is a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") in front of an unlocked chest. As you approach the bandit and chest, a giant frostbite spider will descend from a hole in the ceiling and attack along with any spiders that haven't already been alerted to your presence. The tunnel heading north leads to a small area with some thick cobwebs to the west concealing an unlocked chest, and to the north is a chain that opens a hidden door.

Snapleg Cave hag

Behind the door is another chamber with a single hag in front of a tent. In the tent are three barrels with a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")*, a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random potion of magicka, two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), and three [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") on top. A second tent holds only a dead [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") and two dead [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Just outside this tent are two barrels containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), with a random potion on top of one of them. There are two fly amanita fungus patches and several hanging mosses growing in this chamber. The exit to the next room is to the southwest.

Snapleg's prisoner

A wooden bridge spanning a small stream leads to the last occupied room of the cave. The body of a [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") is in the water to the right of the bridge, but most notably, up ahead a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") is trapped in a cage behind an apprentice lock. A [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") and a hag are in a tent farther back to the south. The spriggan will not turn hostile if you free her, and makes a valuable ally against the enemies. Once the enemies are dispatched, if the spriggan survived, she flees the cave and vanishes at the exit. There is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") to the left of the tent. By the mouth of the tent is a barrel of ingredients with two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top. Inside the tent is a table with two empty random soul gems and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. To the right of the tent, against the cave wall is yet another barrel containing ingredients. To the west a wooden ramp leads up into the final room that contains the alchemy lab, chest, and barrels seen previously. The chest is unlocked and will likely contain your quest target if a radiant quest directed you here, and the barrels contain foodstuffs. The spriggan may be waiting by some spears blocking the way. Use the chain to the right to lower them. Exit onto a ledge overlooking the first encampment, but don't drop down off the ledge; instead, follow it to the right and through to the sinkhole, where you can drop down right by the exit. In front of you is a column that it is possible to jump onto, but apart from being able to jump to reach a hanging moss, there is nothing else of interest on the column.

## Notes

- Snapleg Cave also [appeared](/wiki/Online:Snapleg_Cave "Online:Snapleg Cave") in [Elder Scrolls Online](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").
- Even if not freed from the cage, the peaceful [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") will run to [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary") and stand in the thicket near the swimming hole.
- There is a "Small Bird" (Ref ID: 0009CAE9) hidden inside the wall of the first major chamber of the cave. It can only be seen by clipping through the walls or in the Creation Kit, and is unique to this cave.
- Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") assigns Snapleg Cave to [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") instead.

## Bugs

- One of the goats may be partially glitched into the ground.
- There's a deathbell in a crate in the first room that is incorrectly owned by [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure"). Taking it therefore counts as stealing.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- The spellcaster trap that shoots ice spikes may fire in rapid three-spike volleys (rather than singular spikes, as it should), making it especially deadly. If it happens to be shooting three-spike rounds, it will also be heard shooting at the wall leading up to it, well before you reach it. **?**

## Maps

  Snapleg Cave

# Skyrim:Snow Elf

## Overview

Knight-Paladin Gelebor

The Great Statue of [Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand"), a rare depiction of a Snow Elf

**Snow Elves** (also known as **Ancient Falmer** to distinguish them from their devolved modern counterparts) are a largely extinct race of mer that once inhabited the province of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). They resemble the golden-skinned [Altmer](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") in height and physiognomy though differ in being white-haired, pale, and have very long lifespans, as well as a strong resistance to frost. They worshipped [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El") and built the [Chantry of Auri-El](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)") and various wayshrines in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). Following their defeat at the [Battle of the Moesring](/wiki/Lore:Battle_of_the_Moesring "Lore:Battle of the Moesring"), Snow Elves were the victims of a genocide by the Atmorans that left their numbers significantly low. Many took refuge with the [Dwemer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer "Skyrim:Dwemer"), who in exchange for protection forced them to eat a toxic blinding fungus that turned them into the twisted and primal modern-day [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), known by surviving Snow Elves as "The Betrayed".

For more information, see the [main lore article](/wiki/Lore:Snow_Elf "Lore:Snow Elf").

## Snow Elves

There are a total of seven Snow Elves; only Gelebor is unaffected by a form of undeath, as Vyrthur is also a vampire and the prelates are all ghosts. They are all encountered in the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") [add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Add-ons "Skyrim:Add-ons").

| Name | Location |
| --- | --- |
| [Arch-Curate Vyrthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Curate_Vyrthur "Skyrim:Arch-Curate Vyrthur") | [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)") ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |
| [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor") | [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave") ([The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach")) [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)") ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |
| [Prelate Athring](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Athring "Skyrim:Prelate Athring") | Wayshrine of Sight ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |
| [Prelate Celegriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Celegriath "Skyrim:Prelate Celegriath") | Wayshrine of Learning ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |
| [Prelate Edhelbor](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Edhelbor "Skyrim:Prelate Edhelbor") | Wayshrine of Radiance ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |
| [Prelate Nirilor](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Nirilor "Skyrim:Prelate Nirilor") | Wayshrine of Resolution ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |
| [Prelate Sidanyis](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Sidanyis "Skyrim:Prelate Sidanyis") | Wayshrine of Illumination ([Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")) |

## Related Quests

- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

## Notes

- In the game files, every member is part of a newly-created race known as `SnowElfRace`. It is largely based off of the High Elf race, and even bears the name "High Elf" internally, but for all purposes all members of the race are to be considered Snow Elves.
  - All Snow Elves that can be met, are male. This appears to be a deliberate design decision, as there are no traces of female Snow Elf NPCs ever having been created. In fact, the racial traits of snow white skin and the unique albino white hair color aren't even set up to work with female NPCs, further suggesting they were never meant to exist.
- You cannot harvest [Arch-Curate Vyrthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Curate_Vyrthur "Skyrim:Arch-Curate Vyrthur")'s Snow Elf blood with the [Essence Extractor](/wiki/Skyrim:Essence_Extractor "Skyrim:Essence Extractor") for [Discerning the Trasmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane").
- Wispmothers in Skyrim are believed to be the ghosts of Snow Elves. [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)") is said to have been a foe of [Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor "Skyrim:Ysgramor") named Aumriel.

## Bugs

- [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad")'s damage bonus against elves does not apply to Snow Elves.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.

### Books

- ***[The Betrayed](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Betrayed "Skyrim:The Betrayed")*** by [Engwe Emeloth](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Engwe_Emeloth "Lore:Books by Author") — A poem surrounding the tragic fall of the Snow Elves
- ***[Diary of Faire Agarwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Diary_of_Faire_Agarwen "Skyrim:Diary of Faire Agarwen")*** by [Faire Agarwen](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Faire_Agarwen "Lore:Books by Author") — The ancient diary of a Snow Elf lamenting the extermination of their race
- ***[Fall of the Snow Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_of_the_Snow_Prince "Skyrim:Fall of the Snow Prince")*** by [Lokheim](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Lokheim "Lore:Books by Author") — An account of the Battle of the Moesring as transcribed by Lokheim, chronicler to the chieftain Ingjaldr White-Eye
- ***[The Falmer: A Study](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Falmer:_A_Study "Skyrim:The Falmer: A Study")*** by [Ursa Uthrax](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Ursa_Uthrax "Lore:Books by Author") — A study on Falmer, recounting their war with the Dwemer
- ***[Journal of Mirtil Angoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_of_Mirtil_Angoth "Skyrim:Journal of Mirtil Angoth")*** by [Mirtil Angoth](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Mirtil_Angoth "Lore:Books by Author") — The ancient diary of a Snow Elf and their plan to seek refuge with the Dwemer
- ***[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky_(book) "Skyrim:Touching the Sky (book)")*** by [Parmion Saldor](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Parmion_Saldor "Lore:Books by Author") — An overview of Snow Elf pilgrimages to the Chantry of Auri-El
- ***[The Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wispmother "Skyrim:The Wispmother")*** by [Mathias Etienne](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Mathias_Etienne "Lore:Books by Author") — Summation of legends regarding the Wispmothers

Snow-Shod Farm

**Snow-Shod Farm** is a small farm south of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") that is owned by [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod").

[Addvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvild "Skyrim:Addvild") and [Leonara Arius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leonara_Arius "Skyrim:Leonara Arius") live there and run the farm for Vulwulf.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Addvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvild "Skyrim:Addvild")  [Leonara Arius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leonara_Arius "Skyrim:Leonara Arius") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Snow-Shod Farm

There are two buildings on the lot: a farmhouse and a windmill. In the field, there are four bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") , ten [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and five [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants, all of which [Addvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Addvild "Skyrim:Addvild") will pay you for gathering. There is a [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two patches of [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") mushrooms, a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") all growing in and around the farm. There are also four [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken"), two nests for collecting [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and one [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") that produces [milk](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug_of_Milk "Skyrim:Jug of Milk") all on the farm.

| Crops | Plants | Mushrooms | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 [Gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd")  10 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  5 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato")  4 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") | 2 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") | 4 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Snow-Shod Farm

Snow-Shod Farm interior

Entering the farmhouse brings you straight into the main living room, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand against the northeast wall. Coming out from the southeast wall is a large wooden table with benches either side, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top. There are [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks and barrels all around the farmhouse. On the southwest wall is a wall shelf holding clutter, with a chair against the same wall and a cupboard further to the right of the chair. The cupboard holds a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and three loaves of bread. Above the cupboard, hanging from the ceiling are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). A doorway to the northwest leads to the top of a flight of stairs leading down to the cellar. The stairs descend to the northeast.

Snow-Shod Farm bedroom

At the bottom is a storage area with a pile of firewood and a couple of straw bales under the stairs and against the southwest wall is a set of shelves that hold several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two loaves of bread, several pieces of cheese and a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods")*. There is a dresser to the left, against the southeast wall with a bottle of wine atop. To the left is a doorway through into their bedroom which consists of a double bed coming out from the middle of the southeast wall, with a wall shelf above the bed holding a bottle of alto wine and a dresser at the foot of the bed with a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") on top. In the eastern corner is an end table with a copy of *[Rising Threat, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. IV")*, a chair against the southwest wall and a wardrobe in the northwest corner containing [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing").

## Notes

- The farmyard is one of the common places you can encounter the [revelers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reveler "Skyrim:Reveler").
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the barrels outside the building as owned by the farm.

## Bugs

- The guards at the farm have no patrol route data set up and would thus be standing totally idle 24/7.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Snow-Shod Manor

## Overview

Snow-Shod Manor in Riften

**Snow-Shod Manor** is a large manor in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), home of the Snow-Shod clan. It is located at the northeastern part of Riften, between [Aerin's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin%27s_House "Skyrim:Aerin's House") and [Riftweald Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Riftweald_Manor "Skyrim:Riftweald Manor").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Asgeir Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod")  [Nura Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Nura_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Nura Snow-Shod")  [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod") |

### Snow-Shod Manor

The entrance is kept adept-locked most of the time. Upon entering you are in a large open room with a flight of stairs up on your left, with stairs leading down to the cellar behind and several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and sacks around the stairwell. A long end table is against the north wall, on top of which is a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), as well as a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). There is a chair opposite the entrance against the east wall, with a wall shelf above holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). To the right of the chair is a cupboard and a set of shelves in the southeast corner. These hold a bunch of lavender, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of wine, copies of *[Rising Threat, Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. III")*, *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*, and *[Dwemer Inquiries Vol II](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Inquiries_Vol_II "Skyrim:Dwemer Inquiries Vol II")*, an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a couple sacks. Against the south wall is an end table that holds a bottle of alto wine with a chair on either side, and against the west wall another long end table holding an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk").

Dining room

There is a doorway in the northeast corner leading through into the dining area, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand against the west wall, a cupboard containing only clutter against the north wall, and a wooden dining table and benches in the middle of the room. On the table are three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of alto wine, a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). Hanging from the ceiling are two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the west is the staircase leading down to the cellar.

At the bottom of the stairs, against the south wall is a large pile of firewood and several bales of straw, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against the firewood. To the east is a storage area full of various crates, barrels, and sacks. To the north is another storage area with a disused table and chairs, two sets of shelves, and a cupboard containing clutter. On the shelves are various pieces of cheese, two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a load of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and several loaves of bread. To the right of the cupboard is a small round table holding a mead barrel.

Snow-Shod's bedroom

To the right at the top of the stairs is a landing and corridor, with a bedroom to the east belonging to [Asgeir Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Asgeir_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Asgeir Snow-Shod"), a double bedroom to the west shared by [Vulwulf Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulwulf_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Vulwulf Snow-Shod") and his wife, [Nura Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Nura_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Nura Snow-Shod"), and at the end of the corridor, by some barrels, sacks, and a crate, another bedroom; it would have been their daughter's room, who died after joining the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Lore:Stormcloaks "Lore:Stormcloaks").

Asgeir's bedroom is L-shaped, long, and narrow, and consists of a single owned bed against the east wall, with a small low table beside it. On the table is a bottle of wine. To the right is a chair, and against the west wall is a long end table with an iron sword and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") on top. Opposite the door, against the east wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Lilija's old room consists of a single owned bed against the east wall, with an end table beside it against the north wall, and a wardrobe containing clothes beside that. Against the west wall is an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, and opposite the door is a long end table with a bunch of lavender on top.

The parents' room contains an owned double bed coming out from the south wall, with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and two loose coins underneath, an end table to the left, and a wall shelf above it. On the end table is a copy of *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")*, and on the shelf are two bottles of wine. At the foot of the bed is a long end table, and to the right of the bed is a fireplace. Along the west wall is a pile of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), while in the northwest corner is a small square wooden table and two chairs, with a loaf of bread and a bottle of wine on top of the table. Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe containing clothes.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the right of the entrance door.

# Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Snow Veil Sanctum ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snow+Veil+Sanctum)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No (see [bugs](#Bugs)) |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |

| *[Three Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Three_Thieves "Skyrim:Three Thieves")* *[Ice and Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_and_Chitin "Skyrim:Ice and Chitin")* [Model Ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Model_Ship "Skyrim:Model Ship") | |

| Special Features | |

Just outside of the entrance, with the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") in the background

**Snow Veil Sanctum** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north-northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr").

It contains two zones, *[Snow Veil Catacombs](#Snow_Veil_Catacombs)* and *[Snow Veil Sanctum](#Snow_Veil_Sanctum)*. It is locked and inaccessible prior to the related quest [Speaking With Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence"), during which it is the hideout of [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah"), a supposed murderer and betrayer of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). It is full of leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), and at least one undead boss.

The second zone contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for the [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), making the related quest and its five prerequisite quests necessary to unlock all three words of Disarm.

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[Speaking With Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence")**: Track down the [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") behind the Guild's misfortunes.

### Exterior

During the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence"), there will be a tent, two bedrolls, and Karliah's dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") to the south of the entrance to the ruin. Several random items can be found on the dead horse, including [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"). [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") will be in front of the barrow entrance and will initiate conversation as you approach, confirming he was the one who killed Karliah's horse to prevent her escape. Only Mercer can unlock the door into the ruin, and followers are unable to enter. There are two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks to the left of the entrance, and blood splatters on the ground in front.

There is an alternative entrance to the northwest, but the way is blocked by an impassable gate until you've passed through the entire ruin from the main entrance.

### Snow Veil Catacombs

The interior of the ruin is filled with traps set by [Karliah](/wiki/Skyrim:Karliah "Skyrim:Karliah") for Mercer Frey, as well as the normal traps found in typical barrows, including [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") to wake the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") she also left for you to deal with.

Upon entering, as with many other Nordic ruins, you'll be at the top of a set of narrow stairs. At the bottom of the stairs is a cluster of [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") and an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") on the ground. Continue through the first room and down another flight of stairs to a room containing two [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers"), a pull chain, an apprentice-trapped [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and two ominous upright sarcophagi. Opening the chest without disarming the trap will trigger the sarcophagi to burst open and draugr to attack. There are two gates in the corners of the north wall operated by the chain on the south wall; however, the right-hand gate has a cave-in behind it and won't open. Behind the left-hand gate is an alcove with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random potion of [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on a set of shelves. A doorway to the east descends to the next room.

This room contains several more sarcophagi, all of which are already open with draugr inside. One of these is leveled and only slumbering, but will only wake if you attack it. There are three more dead draugr lying on the ground, and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") in front of a gate in the south wall. There is a chain to the right that opens it, but also triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") to the right. To avoid the spikes, immediately jump back once you pull the chain.

Follow the passage as it takes a turn before reaching a typical catacomb area with upright alcoves and many burial urns; many of the alcoves contain slumbering leveled draugr. The second small section of the catacomb features an adept-locked iron door, beyond which is a small alcove containing a sideboard with a random potion of healing, a random potion of stamina, and two random potions of [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") on top, with an [ancient Nord sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Sword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Sword") and an [ancient Nord war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_War_Axe "Skyrim:Ancient Nord War Axe") on the shelf underneath. There are three [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on the ground in the next small section of the catacomb, and a draugr patrols the next corridor. A total of eight draugr are in this area, many leveled, with two [tripwires](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that cause two nearby [oil lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") to fall to the ground and ignite an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"). A [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") lies against the east wall by the oil slick among some rubble, and to the south is a lowered gate, with the chain that opens it to the left.

Beyond the gate are stairs leading down to a passage with two draugr on guard. A short passage is on the left, and an apprentice-locked door is ahead. There is a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") lying on the ground before the door. Behind the door is a small room containing three large urns, three burial urns on a stone table, an unlocked chest, and an empty set of shelves. There is also a barred opening acting as a window into a two-level room farther ahead, with several leveled draugr and [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") wandering in and out of view. It is advisable to use ranged attacks from here to avoid a potentially difficult fight later. The passage on the left leads into a room with many [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling; around the room are five upright sarcophagi, up to four of which contain slumbering leveled draugr. There is a sideboard to the southeast with the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Three Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Three_Thieves "Skyrim:Three Thieves")* and three random potions on top: one healing, one magicka, and one stamina. To the east is a closed gate, with a chain to the right to open it.

The Model Ship

The passage behind the gate descends several flights of stairs and takes three turns before entering the room seen from the window. As you near the entrance, one of the sarcophagi in the room will burst open, and a magic-using draugr will emerge. There are stone stairs to the right and wooden stairs in front leading up to two balcony areas. Taking the wooden stairs leads up to a balcony with two sarcophagi; one is open and contains a dead draugr, while a set of shelves by the other holds nothing but clutter. Between the two sarcophagi is a passage patrolled by a leveled draugr. The passage eventually leads to a third balcony in the main room, with a [trapped pedestal](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") holding the [Model Ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Model_Ship "Skyrim:Model Ship") that can be sold to Delvin as part of [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny") quest. The pedestal is surrounded by an oil slick, and has an oil lantern hanging above that is dropped when you remove the model. There is a potion of healing, a potion of magicka, a potion of stamina, an ancient Nord sword, an ancient Nord war axe, two [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), and two burial urns on sideboards around this balcony; these items may be blown about if the trap is triggered before you collect them. To avoid damage, leap off the balcony back to the bottom of the room as soon as you take the model. The stone stairs lead to another balcony, with two large urns flanking a passage heading south. This passage climbs and turns to the east, north, and east again. At the end it leads out onto a covered walkway that passes high over the main room below. By a pillar where the walkway turns is a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on the ground by an animal skull. The walkway continues to an iron door, which opens into the second zone, *Snow Veil Sanctum*.

### Snow Veil Sanctum

A barnacle cluster out of water...

The Sanctum opens into more catacombs with the dead laid out in alcoves along the walls, some draugr only slumbering as before. Two draugr sleep on the left, and one sleeps opposite on the right. Sneak attacking any of these is likely to alert all three. There is a [Nordic barnacle cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle Cluster") on the ground just before the three sleeping draugr. Around the corner, stairs descend to an area with two chests opposite each other; one is unlocked, and the other is adept-locked, while each is behind a string of bone chimes. A total of five leveled draugr are in alcoves nearby; again, this can be a difficult fight for the unprepared. Once the draugr have all been dealt with, at the end of the room is another lowered gate, with the chain to open it on the left. Beyond the gate is a brightly lit area, with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") partially concealed beneath pottery that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap").

Around the corner, a narrow passage leads to another leveled draugr and stairs leading up. On the right at the bottom of the stairs is a [burnt corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Burnt Corpse"), with a second burnt corpse at the top lying beside a dead draugr in the middle of the passage. Behind the dead draugr is a pair of open double doors, with a wide passage beyond. At the end is a pair of closed double iron doors. As you approach, Mercer will warn you to be ready, as the door is perfect for hiding an ambush. Opening the door causes two draugr (one of them a boss, which at higher levels may be a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest")) to awaken and burst from their sarcophagi on a raised area in front of you. There is also a sarcophagus at either end of the room to the east and west, with each containing a draugr that will burst forth and attack if you get too close or make too much noise. At the rear of the room behind the central raised section is the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), which teaches a word for the [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). There are wooden stairs leading up to the raised section both in front and behind it, with a stone table to the left of the front stairs holding a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[Ice and Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_and_Chitin "Skyrim:Ice and Chitin")*. There is also an unlocked boss chest on the raised section. To the east is another lowered gate, with the chain to the right.

The passage beyond the gate leads around to a short passage with three bear traps on the ground and a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzles#Dragon_Claw_Switch "Skyrim:Puzzles") at the far end. Mercer will take over and start talking while opening it. This is the only puzzle door in the game without a corresponding [dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Dragon Claw"). Once the door is opened, a cutscene plays.

Should you return after the events of Speaking with Silence, you can traverse the ruin again. The final room is a series of terraces up to an upright sarcophagus, with a lowered gate behind it, and the chain to operate it to the right. Behind the gate is a short passage to an iron door leading outside via the alternative exit. The only thing in the final room after the quest will be a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") on the floor. Outside, flanking the alternative exit are two barrels of ingredients and a food sack. This exit is located west of the main entrance, midway between the main entrance and [Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine"), and cannot be seen from the road.

## Notes

- Followers will never follow you inside, even after completing the quest.
- There is a stone platform west-northwest of the entrance to the Sanctum with an inaccessible grate-covered well in its center. Two [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") will periodically spawn here, and can often be seen fighting with a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") that spawns nearby. The top of the alternative exit can be seen by standing at the northernmost edge of this platform.
- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is southeast of the dungeon, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") can be found northwest of here.
- Setting off the oil lantern traps in the room with the [Model Ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Model_Ship "Skyrim:Model Ship") before picking it up can cause it to be blown off of its pedestal, making it potentially difficult to find again.
  -  Select the Model Ship through the console by entering `prid d32e2`, then type `moveto player` to move it to the player.

## Bugs

- Snow Veil Sanctum cannot be cleared because the boss creature does not have the boss flag.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The containers outside the entrance respawn despite the dungeon being classed as a "no reset zone". **?**

# Skyrim:Snowclad Ruins

## Overview

| Northwest of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") Southeast of [Hrothmund's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrothmund%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Hrothmund's Barrow") | |

Snowclad Ruins

**Snowclad Ruins** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") northwest of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") containing [werebears](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear").

A large pool of water in front of the ruin is fed by an aqueduct from the southwest and empties into a waterfall to the northeast.

## Walkthrough

From [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike"), ascend the nearby slope to the west, then the steps passing under two stone arches on the left to the southeast. The path turns briefly south after the first arch, then southeast again after the second. Climb a final set of steps to reach the top, where you will find a third arch with a dead [reaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") underneath surrounded in gore, blood and bones, and a second dead reaver immediately to the left of the arch. Beyond the arch, a short set of steps descends a slope to the southeast, with a view of the ruin below ahead. To the right of the steps is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush. Follow blood splatters down the slope until you discover another dead reaver slumped by a rock. Here, the path continues to descend to the south via another short set of steps to the edge of the pool in front of the ruins. Beware, as a werebear patrols this area, while another two werebears are near the altar ahead; they will immediately transform and attack when alerted to your presence. The path follows the edge of the pool before passing under the aqueduct.

The altar

The ruin consists of an L-shaped stone foundation, with an altar set in an alcove at its south end. There is a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt") on the ground to the right of the altar, a dead [snow fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox "Skyrim:Snow Fox") on the ground to the left, and a dead [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") on top. Two treasure chests can be found here: one in the pool at the base of the waterfall dropping from the aqueduct, and another on top of the alcove holding the altar. The second can be reached by [climbing](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") the rocks to the right of the altar. Finally, there is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and three [apothecary's satchels](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") (two rare, one common) just east of the ruins. If you are facing the altar, the skeleton is on the rocky ledge to your left, about 100 feet down and around the cliff face.

## Notes

- The altar in the ruin is dedicated to [Hircine](/wiki/Lore:Hircine "Lore:Hircine"), similar to the one found in [Glenmoril Coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Coven "Skyrim:Glenmoril Coven"). It may be a reference to [Hircine's Hunt](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hircine%27s_Hunt "Bloodmoon:Hircine's Hunt"), which has taken place on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim") in the past.

# Skyrim:Snowpoint Beacon

## Overview

| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 5 |
| Occupants | |

| Console Location Code(s) | |

| Southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") East of [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") | |

Snowpoint Beacon

**Snowpoint Beacon** is a small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The main path to the tower approaches from the north, with stone steps leading up to a doorway in the lowest of the tower's three floors. It is also possible to climb the mountain behind [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") to reach the tower from the southwest; from this direction, you will reach the middle floor first.

There is nothing of interest on the lowest floor, which features only a spiral stone staircase leading up to the middle floor. At the top of the stairs is a large hole in the wall leading out onto a wooden platform. A bandit wielding a [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") guards this level. Inside against an internal wall is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot with a mounted wolf head above it. To the left is a stack of crates with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on top. The internal staircase continues to the top floor, where a bandit chief stands looking out to the north, allowing you to attack from behind. A quiver of eighteen random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") rests on a table. To the right of the table is a lean-to with an unowned bedroll under it, and farther to the right are some barrels containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food").

## Notes

- Two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") are east of the tower on a small plateau on the side of the mountain.

## Overview

Solitude Blacksmith

**Solitude Blacksmith** is a smithy in the western side of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

It is worked by [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand") and [Heimvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimvar "Skyrim:Heimvar"). The interior is quite large, and there is a decent number of things that can be stolen. [Heimvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimvar "Skyrim:Heimvar") can usually be found at a grindstone downstairs.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")  [Heimvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimvar "Skyrim:Heimvar") |

### Exterior

The blacksmiths are found within the grounds of [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"), just outside the walls. It is found at the top of a ramp leading up from the market area. From the top of the ramp turn to the right. On the end of the wall separating the ramp from the blacksmiths is a [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)")  "Loot") Loot. To the right of the entrance is a cart containing several [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). Further along is the [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") where Beirand can usually be found working. At the rear, against the wall is a wooden table with several items of Beirand's stock that will disappear when purchased. In addition to the forge there is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") as well as several barrels of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") all around the forge area.

### Solitude Blacksmith

Heimvar working on the grindstone

Upon entering you are in a wide room with a central pillar and a door to the residence opposite. On the right is a firepit, with a stone wall around it. There are three [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on the top of the wall and a grindstone beside it. Above the firepit is a rack holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). On your right as you enter, against the south wall is a barrel containing foodstuffs and eight [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") on top. Beside this is a set of shelves holding several cheese wheels, five potatoes, a cabbage and a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). In an alcove to the east are two large piles of firewood and a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes").

In the northeastern corner are two small units holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). On the north wall are two wall shelves holding fifteen iron ingots, two silver ingots and four [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"). To the left of these is the door to the residence and to the left of that is a small unit containing clothes with a rack holding two [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids. Further along the wall is a barrel of foodstuffs and a set of shelves holding four leather strips and two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") and in the northwestern corner a stack of more barrels containing food.

Through the door into the residence on the left is a set of shelves holding several cheese wheels, a cabbage, five potatoes and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"). On the right is a table and chairs set for two, with two [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), some bread, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a bulb of garlic. Above the table are three wall shelves holding two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), several cups and a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"). Directly opposite the door against the northeast wall is an alcove containing several barrels of food, a table holding two leather strips, three iron ingots and a cabbage, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") underneath and a bale of straw behind. Beside the table is basket containing two cabbages and five potatoes.

Heimvar's room

To the east is a door into Heimvar's bedroom, which contains a tall wardrobe on the right as you enter, against the north wall a narrow table holding an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower and bunch of tundra cotton. Above this is a wall shelf holding three common books. Against the east wall is an empty set of small shelves. There is an unowned single bed in the southeastern corner with a wall shelf above on the east wall holding two leather strips. There is an open crate at the foot of the bed containing a bunch of tundra cotton and to the right of the bed is a table holding a cup.

The stairs up to the top floor are to the west, with a barrel of food on the left of them. At the top of the stairs against the north wall is a small cupboard with a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") on top. Opposite the top of the stairs is a door into Beirand's bedroom. To the right of this is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, with a narrow table to the right of this, holding a bowl of bread, a plate holding a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and an iron dagger. Above these is a wall shelf holding one iron and one steel ingot. Against the south wall is a bookcase holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), nine common books, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). In front of this is a low table and chair holding a common book, a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") of bread and cheese.

Beirand's bedroom consists of a single unowned bed in the southeastern corner, a wardrobe on your left as you enter the room, a small unit against the east wall holding a level-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") and a plate of bread and cheese. In front of this is a low table and chair holding the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), with a wooden bench against the north wall. Further along the wall is a narrow table holding an iron dagger and bowl containing a bunch of tundra cotton. Above this is a wall shelf holding a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts") and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Refugees](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Refugees "Skyrim:The Refugees")*. Against the west wall is a tall set of shelves holding two [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), two bottles of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a deathbell flower, a bowl of void salts and a basket containing two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender").

### Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the blacksmith's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Notes

- In [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online"), [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Online:Radiant_Raiment "Online:Radiant Raiment") was located in this building.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this shop is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.

## Bugs

- The Blacksmith sign when ran and jumped into may make you suddenly end up in a large body of water with nothing around you. When checked on the map it tilts the map upwards as if you were in the sky. Has also occurred on Playstation 3 and can be fast traveled away from.
- [Heimvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimvar "Skyrim:Heimvar") is officially the backup blacksmith for Solitude Blacksmith. However, Heimvar is not set up properly, meaning that if [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand") dies there is no longer anyone who will provide blacksmith merchant services in Solitude.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Solitude Blacksmith isn't correctly flagged as a store or dwelling, and is also missing the TGBusiness keyword for Thieves Guild radiant quests even though it has all the required parts in place.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Solitude Catacombs

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cemetery: Solitude Catacombs ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Catacombs)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SolitudeHalloftheDeadCatacombs | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | |

Solitude Catacombs

**Solitude Catacombs** is an area occupied by [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") which can be accessed either via the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") or directly from the city.

Inside the catacombs

## Related Quests

- **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")**: Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.
- **[Return to Grace](/wiki/Skyrim:Return_to_Grace "Skyrim:Return to Grace")**: Convince a mourning [mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta") to go to the [local temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines").

### Exterior

The catacombs are in the building behind the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)"), with an underground doorway linking the two. There is a small graveyard containing a dozen gravestones outside in front of the entrance, with four nightshade plants among them. There is a short flight of stairs down to the door.

### Solitude's Catacombs

Entering from the outside, you find yourself at the top of a flight of stairs heading northwest, with typical Nord catacombs ahead. There are many [hanging mosses](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from the walls throughout the catacombs, with many ingredients left as offerings in addition to loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a couple bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Standing at the far end by a junction is a melee [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). The path splits to the northeast and southwest, before both paths turn back to head northwest again and climb parallel sets of stairs. At the top of the stairs, both paths turn again to complete a square. In the top corners are two more melee skeletons. At the other end of the catacombs, directly opposite the initial entrance, is the second entrance from the Hall of the Dead. The burial urns found here are unique to this location; however, they are all empty.

## Ingredients

| Ingredients |
| --- |
| 6 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  73 [Hanging Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss")  2 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes")  8 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")  6 [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing")  6 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  1 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota")  12 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries")  1 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton")  1 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") |

## Gallery

- 

  One type of coffin
- 

  Another type of coffin

## Notes

- After [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir")'s execution, his body will be buried here in accordance with Nord tradition at the request of [Styrr](/wiki/Skyrim:Styrr "Skyrim:Styrr"), priest of Arkay.
- The location contains many Hanging Moss. They are marked "Steal", but there is no consequence for taking them. The owner appears to be Styrr. After becoming friends with Styrr (completing the Wolf Queen Awakened quest) they will no longer be marked "Steal" (similar to the garlic braids in the Hall of the Dead).
- In the quest Bound Until Death, if the corpse of [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") disappears from the wedding location quest area due to the player fast traveling or for another reason, it can subsequently be found in the catacombs.
- Going through the door from the graveyard to the Catacombs turns the direction of the player from southeast to northwest. This orientation is appropriate to make the Catacombs link up with the Hall of the Dead at the other end. If the steps down to the door were behind Jala's House, the orientations on both side of the door would have been appropriate.

# Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse

## Overview

Solitude Lighthouse

**Solitude Lighthouse** is a stone building on the northern coast of Skyrim that helps to guide ships into Solitude harbor. It is tended to by a Khajiit named [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka"), who lives here alone.

Solitude Lighthouse at night

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka") |

## Related Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.

### Exterior

There are several [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants and a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") nearby. Directly west of the [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), in the small cavity of the rock formation is a bottle of [Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") and an [Empty Skooma Bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Skooma_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Skooma Bottle"). They are somewhat difficult to see due to the gravel texture of the ground. The [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") depicted in [Treasure Map III](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_III "Skyrim:Treasure Map III") is to the northeast, under the cliff edge. As you pass through the outer archway there is a door on your left that leads to the interior, which may be apprentice-locked. Continuing through the inner arch you come to a long spiral stone staircase that leads all the way up to the top and the fire that acts as the light for ships.

### Solitude Lighthouse

Ma'zaka sitting in the residence

Through the door on the left, you enter what appears to be a normal house, with barrels of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") on either side of you, with a wooden table further to the left against the south wall. On the table is a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). Against the west wall is a set of shelves holding several cheese wheels, two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). To the right is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a piece of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and a cabbage in a cast iron pot on the hearth. To the right of the fireplace, coming out from the west wall is an internal wall. There is a plate holding [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") on top of it, and a stack of two open crates on the floor beside it containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and two loaves of bread.

Along the east wall are two stacked open crates containing a sample of fly amanita, a gourd, a rock warbler egg and an orange dartwing, three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and two potatoes. To the left of these is a set of shelves holding eight [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). Further to the left, still against the east wall are two more stacked crates containing a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), six [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs, four [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), and a cabbage. A small set of shelves next to these holds two potatoes, a portion of grilled leeks, two loaves of bread, a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") breast and a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). Hanging above these are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

Behind the internal wall is a table and chairs set for two, with two portions of grilled leeks, two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a loaf of bread, an eidar cheese wedge, and a bulb of garlic. Above the table on the west wall is a wall shelf holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Against the north wall, next to the table, is a small set of shelves holding a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Lunar Lorkhan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lunar_Lorkhan "Skyrim:The Lunar Lorkhan")*. To the right of this is a doorway into Ma'zaka's bedroom, which consists of a single unowned bed with an end table holding a common book and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") beside the bed and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed. On your right as you enter the room is a small unit holding a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), a [cave bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), and a basket containing two bunches of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). To the left in the northeast corner is a stack of barrels containing foodstuffs.

## Notes

- If the fire here is extinguished, the lighthouse will never be re-lit. If you place torches into the fire pit and travel to somewhere else, the torches and the lighthouse beacon will be lit once you return. However, when viewed from a distance, there will still be no visible light.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, fixes this bug.

## Bugs

- A seemingly defined area stretching from the ship to the south up to just northwest of the lighthouse and east of the rocks may cause the game to crash upon entry.
  - Waiting 31 days for the world cell to reset may resolve this.

# Skyrim:Solitude Military Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Solitude Military Camp

**Solitude Military Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") set up west of [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm") for the [attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") on [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

The camp only appears during the [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") in the Stormcloaks questline.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") |

## Related Quests

- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Solitude Military Camp

It features several small tents, which contain no bed rolls or hay piles. Several tree stumps are scattered in the area, with two being [wood chopping blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). In the middle of the camp is a table holding iron weapons, which are free to take, as well as an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). Down to the west are most of the tents, a campfire, and one of the wood chopping blocks. Up the hill is another campfire, the other wood chopping block, two small tents, and one large empty tent. To the east of the camp, two catapults are aimed at Solitude.

After the Battle for Solitude, the camp will be disbanded, and its marker will be removed from the world map.

## Notes

- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found east of the camp.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

# Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill

## Overview

|  |
