.jpg)

Solitude Sawmill

**Solitude Sawmill** is a wood mill southwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). It consists of a house and a sawmill. It is owned by [Hjorunn](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjorunn "Skyrim:Hjorunn"), a Nord who employs an Orc named [Kharag gro-Shurkul](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharag_gro-Shurkul "Skyrim:Kharag gro-Shurkul"). You can sell firewood to Hjorunn, and also buy [sawn logs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") here after installing [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") by speaking to Kharag gro-Shurkul.

.jpg)

The house

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Hjorunn](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjorunn "Skyrim:Hjorunn")  [Kharag gro-Shurkul](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharag_gro-Shurkul "Skyrim:Kharag gro-Shurkul") |

## Related Quests

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The path leading to the mill has several [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") along it. There are two garden plots containing a total of fifteen [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and 20 [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants. Alongside the house are several barrels and sacks all containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), towards the rear of the house are two chicken nests containing [eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). Beside the mill is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). Along the shore just downstream of the mill is a second grindstone, two food barrels, a table on which are three [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a firepit with an empty pot over it. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") creation installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found on the shore near the firepit. The path continues past this and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") a few feet further along, then passes a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit") [HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") to a small damaged jetty where a small boat has been moored. Inside the boat is a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and bucket containing three [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). A [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") is on top of a post at the end of the jetty. Another clay deposit is on a small island southwest of the sawmill.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 15 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  20 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Solitude Sawmill

Solitude Sawmill interior

Upon entering there is a half-height internal wall on your left and two open crates along the northeast wall containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), four [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). On the other side of the internal wall is a table holding two potatoes, two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and several pieces of cheese. Under the table are two open crates containing a sample of fly amanita, a gourd, a rock warbler egg, an orange dartwing, three leeks and two potatoes. Beside the table is a basket containing potatoes and two cabbages. Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding several cheese wheels, two loaves of bread, a cabbage, and a potato. To the right of this is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front. On the hearth is a piece of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and a cabbage in a cast iron pot. There is a second interior wall to the right of the fireplace with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") holding a portion of grilled leeks on top. There is a rack holding three garlic braids hanging from the ceiling.

Against the northeast wall are the stairs up to the top floor. Under the stairs are a set of shelves holding two potatoes and a cupboard holding a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and a woodcutter's axe. To the left are two barrels and sacks of foodstuffs. In the western corner of the building is a bedroom with a single unowned bed with an end table beside it. Behind the internal half-height wall beside the fireplace is a table and chairs set for two with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two portions of grilled leeks, two seared slaughterfish, a loaf of bread, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a bulb of garlic.

At the top of the stairs is a wooden bench, with a table and two chairs to the left, in the western corner. On the table is a loaf of bread and bottle of wine. Above the table is a wall shelf holding three copies of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*. Against the southwest wall is a small unit holding two [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a plate, a common book and an unlocked display cabinet containing an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Beside the unit is a sack. The top floor only covers half of the building and has a railing around it. In the southern corner is a second single unowned bed with an end table beside it and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed.

## Notes

- The [key to the millhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Key to Solitude Sawmill") is carried by Hjorunn and Kharag.
- Unlike most other houses, it is locked with a novice-level lock during the day, but unlocked at night.

## Bugs

- The keys to "Hjorunn's room" and "Kharag's room" don't unlock anything, as there are no doors within the mill.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. The keys are removed from their inventories.

| [Elytra](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph"), [Corrupted Spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"), [Skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Sword of Jyggalag](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_Jyggalag "Skyrim:Sword of Jyggalag") *[Spell Tome: Conjure Golden Saint Archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Conjure_Golden_Saint_Archer "Skyrim:Spells")* *[Spell Tome: Conjure Golden Saint Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Conjure_Golden_Saint_Warrior "Skyrim:Spells")* *[Spell Tome: Conjure Dark Seducer Archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Conjure_Dark_Seducer_Archer "Skyrim:Spells")* *[Spell Tome: Conjure Dark Seducer Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells#Conjure_Dark_Seducer_Warrior "Skyrim:Spells")* [Madness Helmet of Recovery](/wiki/Skyrim:Madness_Helmet_of_Recovery "Skyrim:Madness Helmet of Recovery") [Ring of Disrobing](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Disrobing "Skyrim:Ring of Disrobing") [Sheogorath-Shaped Amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped_Amber "Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped Amber") *[Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| ccBGSSSE025RootDungeon | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| Underneath [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | |

Solitude Sewers entrance

**Solitude Sewers** is a sewer system located in western Solitude, overrun with [Sheogorath](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath "Skyrim:Sheogorath")'s influence. The sewers are being encroached upon by a [root tunnel](/wiki/Lore:Root "Lore:Root") from the [Shivering Isles](/wiki/Lore:Shivering_Isles "Lore:Shivering Isles"). The sewers themselves are inaccessible until starting [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order"). It is inhabited by [Elytra](/wiki/Skyrim:Elytra_Nymph "Skyrim:Elytra Nymph") and [Corrupted Spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") resembling [Gnarls](/wiki/Lore:Gnarl "Lore:Gnarl").

Be sure to loot the many [hollowed stumps](/wiki/Skyrim:Hollowed_Stump "Skyrim:Hollowed Stump") throughout the dungeon, as they usually contain [amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber "Skyrim:Amber"), a rare material needed to craft amber arms and armor. Right before reaching [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron")'s lair, you will discover a bunch of [Golden](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden "Skyrim:Golden") and [Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark "Skyrim:Dark") equipment scattered around. A [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_Strange_Arms_and_Armor "Skyrim:Note on Strange Arms and Armor") on the barrel next to the battlefield will reveal that this was the site of a battle between rival [Golden Saints](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Saint "Skyrim:Golden Saint") and [Dark Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Seducer "Skyrim:Dark Seducer"), and that the [Saint](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_Bandit "Skyrim:Saints Bandit") and [Seducer bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Seducers_Bandit "Skyrim:Seducers Bandit") took their equipment from this site. Further along is Thoron's lair, where you will find that he is conducting a ritual with the [Sword of Jyggalag](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword_of_Jyggalag "Skyrim:Sword of Jyggalag"). He is a tough opponent, but after slaying him, his [journals](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Thoron's Journal") reveal that madness had already taken root underneath Solitude, as these root tunnels were already here when Thoron took residence. He only deepened the breach between [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") and the Shivering Isles by using the Sword in his attempt to return to the Isles.

After killing Thoron, be sure to loot the nearby table of the rare [madness ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Madness_Ore "Skyrim:Madness Ore") which is needed for another [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Nerveshatter_(quest) "Skyrim:Nerveshatter (quest)") and the unique [Sheogorath-Shaped Amber](/wiki/Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped_Amber "Skyrim:Sheogorath-Shaped Amber"). Additionally, be sure to read the *[Note on Amber and Madness Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_Amber_and_Madness_Ore "Skyrim:Note on Amber and Madness Ore")* to obtain a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Amber_and_Madness_Smithing "Skyrim:Amber and Madness Smithing") to unlock the secrets of forging madness and amber gear. There's also an Alteration skill book *[Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods")* next to Thoron's cot.

## Related Quests

- **[Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put an end to the melding of planes under [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

## Notes

- The dungeon ambient track "Wind from the Depths" from the *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")* [soundtrack](/wiki/Oblivion:Music "Oblivion:Music") plays while in this dungeon.
- The root tunnel dungeon tile set this dungeon uses was added to the base game and is fully available as a modder's resource.[[1]](#cite_note-SaintsandSeducers-1)

## Bugs

-  The "Wind from the Depths" track does not play in the Solitude Sewers. **?**
- The plants here are unaffected by the [Green Thumb](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Thumb "Skyrim:Green Thumb") perk.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.
- The Note on Strange Arms and Armor and the Note on Amber and Madness Ore both respawn when the dungeon itself does.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Solitude Stables

## Overview

Solitude Stables

**Solitude Stables** is the [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") serving the city of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Located at [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm"), a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") can be bought from [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund") for 1000 gold. If Geimund dies, [Horm](/wiki/Skyrim:Horm "Skyrim:Horm") will instead sell you the stables' horses.

## Related Quests

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Horse Whisperer](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Whisperer "Skyrim:Horse Whisperer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Residents

| Solitude Stables People |
| --- |
| [Fridrika](/wiki/Skyrim:Fridrika "Skyrim:Fridrika")  [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund") [Hostler](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Hostler")  [Horm](/wiki/Skyrim:Horm "Skyrim:Horm") |

## Exterior

The stables use the north end of the yard shared with [Katla's farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm"). There are three steps up to the front door, which isn't locked during the day. Most of the plants and mushrooms can be found against the walls of either the building or stables. There are many barrels of food in the yard.

| Crops | Plants | Mushrooms | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 5 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  2 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  3 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  1 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") | 2 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  2 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat")  2 [Horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

## Solitude Stables

Solitude Stables

On your left when entering is an open crate against the southeast wall containing containing five [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Above this is a rack holding two [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). There is a table against the southwest wall holding two potatoes, a haunch of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), several cheese wheels and wedges, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Under the table is an open crate containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"). To the right is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front. On the hearth is a piece of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), a haunch of venison and a cabbage in a cast iron pot.

There is a round wooden table and two chairs in the middle of the room holding a loaf of bread. There are two racks hanging from the ceiling holding four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). To the right of the fireplace is a cupboard holding four [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), several loaves of bread a haunch of venison, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a couple of cheese wheels, and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). To the northwest is a doorway to a bedroom, with a stack of three barrels between the cupboard and doorway.

Against the northeast wall is a small unit holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a wall shelf holding various [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"). Also against this wall is the staircase leading to the top floor. Under the stairs is a cupboard holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a couple of sacks. To the left is a set of shelves holding several cheese wheels, three cabbages, three potatoes and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"). To the left of this is a second bedroom containing an unowned single bed in the northern corner, with an unlocked chest at the foot of the bed. To the left of the bed is an end table holding a common book. In the southern corner of the room is a stack of three more barrels. The first bedroom contains a single bed in the western corner with an end table to the right.

At the top of the stairs, against the northwest wall, is a small unit holding a selection of [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"), and [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") and a sack. To the left is a small table and two chairs. On the table is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") and a level-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing a considerable amount of gold and a steel ingot. The upstairs only extends halfway across the building, with a railing around the edge. Against the railing is an unowned single bed with an end table to the right and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed.

## Notes

- One [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found behind the goat pen.

## Bugs

- If you buy a horse from here and the horse is killed, attempting to purchase a new horse from the same stable results in 1000 gold being deducted, and [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund") stating that your horse is "the one with the saddle", despite no saddled horse appearing at the stables here. Instead, your new horse spawns at the [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The horses here are able to be taken for free if you befriend anyone in the [SolitudeStablesFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:SolitudeStablesFaction "Skyrim:SolitudeStablesFaction"), due to the horses being owned by the stables faction specifically. The problem is that horses cost 1,000 gold, making them way too valuable to let stablemasters let you ride them for free after completing a small favor.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19062)) The ownership of the horses was changed to just Geimund, rather than the faction, preventing this issue.

Solitude, capital of Skyrim

The view from Solitude's port

Solitude at street level

**Solitude** is a major city on the northwest coast of Skyrim, and the capital of both [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") and the entire province. It is the largest city in Skyrim and seat of the province's High King, and is built on a natural arch over the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Lore:Sea_of_Ghosts "Lore:Sea of Ghosts"). The ruler of Solitude is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), widow to the late [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"), with her throne in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

The city houses many important buildings, including the [headquarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in Skyrim, the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"), and the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). The [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") is also near Solitude.

When you enter Solitude for the first time, [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir") is executed for treason.

For more information on Solitude, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Solitude "Lore:Solitude").

[^a](#note_market)This person only sells goods at the market.

[^b](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^c](#note_nohead)This person is executed upon first entering Solitude.

[^d](#note_wedding)This person only appears during [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death").

#### Daedric

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion")**: Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)")**: Find the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").

#### Side Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.
- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

#### Main Quest

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") capital and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

#### Creation Club

- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put an end to the melding of planes under Solitude.
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.
- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

## Notes

- [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 25,000 gold.
- 6 health potions (3 standard, 2 plentiful, and 1 minor) can be found at certain points around the city. You can take all 6 aforementioned potions for free, and they all respawn every 10 days.
- [Hawks](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk "Skyrim:Hawk") can be seen circling the sky above the city. You can kill them for their [beaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Beak "Skyrim:Hawk Beak") and [feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers"), both of which are alchemy ingredients.
- Solitude also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Solitude "Arena:Solitude")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Solitude "Online:Solitude").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") and [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra")'s conversation only takes place if the player never enters the related area, the time doesn't matter.

## Bugs

- With the Skyrim Special Edition a door to "Quick Test Cell" can be seen on the local map near the entrance to the city. This door is otherwise invisible and can't be interacted with. It is a placeholder door for the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") which changes it to an entrance to the [Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers"). Without the Creation it is just an exit from the [CTest](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#CTest "Skyrim:Test Cells") cell. **?**

Solitude, capital of Skyrim

The view from Solitude's port

Solitude at street level

**Solitude** is a major city on the northwest coast of Skyrim, and the capital of both [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") and the entire province. It is the largest city in Skyrim and seat of the province's High King, and is built on a natural arch over the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Lore:Sea_of_Ghosts "Lore:Sea of Ghosts"). The ruler of Solitude is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), widow to the late [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"), with her throne in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

The city houses many important buildings, including the [headquarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in Skyrim, the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"), and the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). The [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") is also near Solitude.

When you enter Solitude for the first time, [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir") is executed for treason.

For more information on Solitude, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Solitude "Lore:Solitude").

[^a](#note_market)This person only sells goods at the market.

[^b](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^c](#note_nohead)This person is executed upon first entering Solitude.

[^d](#note_wedding)This person only appears during [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death").

#### Daedric

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion")**: Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)")**: Find the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").

#### Side Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.
- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

#### Main Quest

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") capital and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

#### Creation Club

- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put an end to the melding of planes under Solitude.
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.
- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

## Notes

- [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 25,000 gold.
- 6 health potions (3 standard, 2 plentiful, and 1 minor) can be found at certain points around the city. You can take all 6 aforementioned potions for free, and they all respawn every 10 days.
- [Hawks](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk "Skyrim:Hawk") can be seen circling the sky above the city. You can kill them for their [beaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Beak "Skyrim:Hawk Beak") and [feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers"), both of which are alchemy ingredients.
- Solitude also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Solitude "Arena:Solitude")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Solitude "Online:Solitude").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") and [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra")'s conversation only takes place if the player never enters the related area, the time doesn't matter.

## Bugs

- With the Skyrim Special Edition a door to "Quick Test Cell" can be seen on the local map near the entrance to the city. This door is otherwise invisible and can't be interacted with. It is a placeholder door for the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") which changes it to an entrance to the [Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers"). Without the Creation it is just an exit from the [CTest](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#CTest "Skyrim:Test Cells") cell. **?**

Solitude, capital of Skyrim

The view from Solitude's port

Solitude at street level

**Solitude** is a major city on the northwest coast of Skyrim, and the capital of both [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") and the entire province. It is the largest city in Skyrim and seat of the province's High King, and is built on a natural arch over the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Lore:Sea_of_Ghosts "Lore:Sea of Ghosts"). The ruler of Solitude is [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), widow to the late [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"), with her throne in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

The city houses many important buildings, including the [headquarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in Skyrim, the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"), and the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). The [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") is also near Solitude.

When you enter Solitude for the first time, [Roggvir](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggvir "Skyrim:Roggvir") is executed for treason.

For more information on Solitude, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Solitude "Lore:Solitude").

[^b](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^c](#note_nohead)This person is executed upon first entering Solitude.

[^d](#note_wedding)This person only appears during [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death").

#### Daedric

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

#### Imperial Legion

- **[Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion")**: Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)")**: Find the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").

#### Side Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.
- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

| Giver Location | Quest Giver | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |

#### Main Quest

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

#### Stormcloaks

- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") capital and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

#### Creation Club

- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put an end to the melding of planes under Solitude.
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.
- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

## Notes

- [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 25,000 gold.
- 6 health potions (3 standard, 2 plentiful, and 1 minor) can be found at certain points around the city. You can take all 6 aforementioned potions for free, and they all respawn every 10 days.
- [Hawks](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk "Skyrim:Hawk") can be seen circling the sky above the city. You can kill them for their [beaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Beak "Skyrim:Hawk Beak") and [feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers"), both of which are alchemy ingredients.
- Solitude also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Solitude "Arena:Solitude")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Solitude "Online:Solitude").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Sorex Vinius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorex_Vinius "Skyrim:Sorex Vinius") and [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra")'s conversation only takes place if the player never enters the related area, the time doesn't matter.

## Bugs

- With the Skyrim Special Edition a door to "Quick Test Cell" can be seen on the local map near the entrance to the city. This door is otherwise invisible and can't be interacted with. It is a placeholder door for the [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") which changes it to an entrance to the [Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers"). Without the Creation it is just an exit from the [CTest](/wiki/Skyrim:Test_Cells#CTest "Skyrim:Test Cells") cell. **?**

The final battle

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth") about the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") infestation.
2. Clear [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole") of draugr.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Outside the mine, Perth will stop you and say that the mine is closed until the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") sends a group to clear out the draugr that infest it, but has given up hope of that ever happening. To complete the quest, enter the sinkhole and clear out the draugr.

Upon entering the mine, you'll come to a junction. The left branch leads to a dead end area with three draugr and two moonstone ore veins. Up a ramp is the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Jornibret's Last Dance](/wiki/Skyrim:Jornibret%27s_Last_Dance "Skyrim:Jornibret's Last Dance")*, as well as some loose [moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") on a table.

Heading back to the junction and down the right-hand passage takes you to a large, unclimbable sinkhole. There is one moonstone vein located directly before the sinkhole as well. When dropping down the sinkhole, prepare for a tough fight, as three leveled draugr will converge on you upon reaching the bottom. A fourth draugr will arrive later as well. A few [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") potions can be found along the passage leading to the next chamber, whose exit is blocked by a gate, and which contains three levers and another leveled draugr. Pull the left and right levers to open the gate and head up the spiral ramp; pulling the center lever will trigger a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap").

The next chamber is accessed through a set of doors; a pressure plate right before them triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap"). Three leveled draugr inhabit this next chamber, the left side of which is floored with wooden planks covering a small pool containing an unlocked chest. Other loot in this room includes alchemical ingredients, some leveled armor, and two blocks of [refined moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Moonstone "Skyrim:Refined Moonstone") in a bookcase.

The passage behind the doors ascends a flight of stairs, then winds deeper into the dungeon. A small, dark passage at the top of the stairs leads to a small room containing a leveled chest. A pressure plate just past the doors has no apparent effect.

The final chamber consists of a moderately-sized open room, with a stone bier flanked by two statues, and houses a boss-level draugr. The right-hand statue will periodically glow with a green hue, which will heal the boss draugr, while the left-hand statue will periodically glow red, then shoot a fireball at you. This behavior ceases upon the boss draugr's destruction. To the left of the bier is an opening leading to a balcony, which contains a small passage leading back to the sinkhole chamber. Treasure in this room includes some ingredients on the bier and a boss chest behind it. On the way out, there are some ingredients and a leveled weapon resting on a pedestal, as well as two moonstone veins, one to the right of the table and one on the opposite side of the room.

Return to Perth for a cash reward and his gratitude. He will also buy any moonstone ore you have acquired, should you wish to sell it.

## Notes

- The boss level draugr in the final chamber can be quite a challenge, owing to his ability to heal himself and use magic to disarm any weapon that you may wield. However, he will not leave the chamber, which you can use to your advantage. While still in the access tunnel leading to the chamber, it's possible to sneak to the end of the tunnel and use a ranged attack to hit him in the back before he even knows you're there. Once he does turn around and head toward you, retreat back down the tunnel to a safe distance, firing at him the whole time. A useful tactic is to lure him toward you (while in the safety of the tunnel) and use a full [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to knock him down, then pummel him with arrows.
- At higher levels, the boss may be a dragon priest.
- It is possible to enter the ruins through the passage which is used to leave the boss' chamber, not having to jump down the sinkhole. In order to do so, you have to climb the rocks surrounding the sinkhole and use [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to reach the rock shelf, opening your way to the chamber where boss awaits. This leads to a possibility of defeating the boss without getting past the other enemies. If you do so, the quest will end and you'll receive a journal entry telling that the mine is clear, even though you didn't even see the rest of the draugr residing there. If you want to crawl through the whole dungeon, though, you have to use the sinkhole, as you would be unable to open the lever gate from the other side.

## Bugs

- The spear trap in front of the door at the top of the spiral ramp seems to be missing its graphic. Stepping on the pressure plate opens the door to the next chamber, the spear trap sound is heard (activating and resetting), you are damaged, but no visual spears are seen extending from the holes in the walls.
- The draugr respawn, making the quest repeatable and possibly killing the miners should you enter while they're at work.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- On the PS3 version, when you decide to sell some moonstone ore to Perth, he won't speak at all, but will take the ore anyway and you will get your money still **?**
- If the mine is cleared before starting the quest, Perth will be stuck engaging in conversation with the player, telling them about the mine being dangerous, and the quest never starts **?**

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformSoljundsSinkholeA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformSoljundsSinkholeA`.

Soljund's Sinkhole

**Soljund's Sinkhole** is a small [moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone "Skyrim:Moonstone") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") and [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") east of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") initially containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). The mine contains only one zone, *[Soljund's Sinkhole](#Soljund.27s_Sinkhole)*; the settlement's residence is detailed on a [separate page](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_House "Skyrim:Miner's House").

A draugr infestation in the mine caused the miners to flee outside, where you can obtain a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole_(quest) "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole (quest)") from [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth") to drive them out. After the quest is completed, Perth will [buy moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Soljund's Sinkhole Residents

| [Miner's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_House "Skyrim:Miner's House") |
| --- |
| [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth")  [Tuthul](/wiki/Skyrim:Tuthul "Skyrim:Tuthul") |

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole_(quest) "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole (quest)")**: Defeat the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") in Soljund's Sinkhole.

### Exterior

Outside the mine is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") beside a tree stump with a patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus growing on it. To the northeast is the [miner's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_House "Skyrim:Miner's House"). In the rocks above the mine is a tree growing out of a solid rock. Several [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") grow around the miner's house, and two [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants grow to the left of the mine entrance.

### Soljund's Sinkhole

The mine is fairly small, spanning just two caves infested with a few fairly weak draugr. However, you will find it has broken through into a draugr catacomb. You will have to jump in and find an alternate route back out. The draugr in the catacomb are more powerful than those in the mine.

Upon entering you will find that it is sporadically lit, so a light source or spell is recommended to those without any form of night vision. There are quite a few [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and barrels and sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") found throughout the mine. The entrance tunnel descends to the north. At the bottom is a T-junction with several bales of straw in front.

To the west is a cave containing three draugr, one at the bottom and two farther up an earthen ramp near some wooden planking. There is a moonstone ore vein on the ground to the right as you enter, with a bucket containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") in front next to some barrels. To the south is a second ore vein on the ground near a table that has a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on it. Behind the table is the earthen ramp leading up to a raised platform with a straw bale and table on top. On the bales is a piece of [moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore"), with two more pieces on the table along with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Jornibret's Last Dance](/wiki/Skyrim:Jornibret%27s_Last_Dance "Skyrim:Jornibret's Last Dance")*.

To the east the tunnel then turns to the north before opening into a cave with the sinkhole in the middle where the floor has collapsed through into the ancient catacombs, with another ore vein on the ground on the right as you enter. The only way forwards is to drop into the hole, where there is a beam partway down that can be used to arrest your fall and avoid injury. Upon dropping to the bottom, two upright sarcophagi against the south wall will burst open and two draugr will attack and be joined by a third leveled draugr from the north. There is also a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton_(dead) "Skyrim:Breton (dead)") lying at the bottom of the sinkhole among the rubble and an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") against the east wall. Beyond a pair of doorways to the north, there is a cave-in to the west and a corridor into the catacombs heading east. Any noisy fighting will alert another leveled draugr to your presence. At the end there is a doorway to the north, with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") in alcoves on either side. The room ahead has a lever in the center with two more, one on the wall to the east and the other on a wall to the west, with a gated doorway to the north. Beside the lever to the east is an alcove with a dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") laid out. Activating the center lever will trigger a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"), while pulling either of the other levers will raise the gate and allow you to proceed.

Beyond the gate is a wooden spiral staircase climbing up one floor to a corridor heading west that is trapped by a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in front of an iron door. The plate triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the side walls. If the trap is triggered this will alert a leveled draugr in the room through the doors. This next chamber has a central rectangular pool with steps down into it on all sides. There is a long stone table to the north of it, with three dead draugr, a few burial urns and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top. The wall to the north has two upright sarcophagi against it, which will burst open releasing two more draugr to attack. To the south of the pool there is a smaller stone table with a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a [Falmer ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and a leveled [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") potion on top, among loads of candles on stands. There is also a food barrel and a burial urn beside the table, and a flooded hole in the floor to the west. Against the south wall is a set of shelves holding two [refined moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Moonstone "Skyrim:Refined Moonstone") ingots, a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a copy of a rarer book, five common books and (if you have reached level 24) there is a copy of *[Boethiah's Proving](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Proving "Skyrim:Boethiah's Proving")* which will initiate a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling") to find the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"). To the west there are a double wooden door with an urn to the right and a set of shelves to the left holding two more common books. Diving into the hole west of the table allows you to access a flooded chamber under the floor, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") a few paces to the north of the hole, in an alcove to the west.

The double doors open to reveal a flight of stairs leading up with a pressure plate in front that doesn't appear to trigger anything. At the top of the stairs, by a broken urn there is a small tunnel to the west and a slightly larger one to the south. The tunnel to the west is quite short and opens into a corridor with a doorway to the north into a chamber with a chest on a raised section flanked by more candles on stands. It is not locked or trapped and contains minor loot.

The tunnel to the south is much longer and it twists and turns before opening into the final chamber. There is a balcony to the south and east, while the final boss (a high-level draugr or even a [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest")) is around the corner to the west behind an altar. They are flanked by two statues. The one to the left will periodically glow red and shoot a [firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") at you regardless of whether you are [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") and undetected, while the one to the right will glow green and heal the draugr. This can lead to a difficult fight. Once the draugr is defeated the statues will stop glowing allowing you to explore the chamber. There is a moonstone ore vein to the right of the balcony on the south wall, and another on the north wall, to the right of the altar.

On the altar there is a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), an [ancient Nord war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_War_Axe "Skyrim:Ancient Nord War Axe"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and one of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), while behind the altar is an unlocked boss chest. To the left is an earthen ramp leading up to the balcony above the chamber. At the rear of the balcony is a sideboard with a random enchanted [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), a [briar heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart"), and a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"). Northeast of the sideboard is an urn beside a tunnel, but if you head north along the edge of the balcony there is a second large urn. The tunnel takes you up to another ledge above the top of the sinkhole giving you access to the mine and the exit.

## Notes

- If you want to maximize the amount of moonstone obtainable from this mine, you'll be better off if you don't finish the quest Soljund's Sinkhole. If you clear the mine and finish the quest, you can mine 15 moonstone ore every 10 days afterward. If you don't clear the mine and simply stick to mining the three ore veins that are accessible before you jump down the sinkhole, you can mine 27 moonstone ore in 10 days instead.
- If you wish to travel through the mine in reverse, it's possible to [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") across the sinkhole pit by climbing onto the ledge opposite the boss chamber exit, though you can only get as far as the gated door at the spiral staircase. However, this makes it impossible to collect all moonstone ores and ingots, as some areas will be skipped.
- In the quest script `QF_FreeformSoljundsSinkholeA_0006136B` , there's a commented-out debug message that reads *"[Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") needs to activate Soljund's Sinkhole Mine's destructible resource object."* The "destructible resource object" mentioned here is a leftover of the larger vision for the Civil War, which would have seen you sent on missions to sabotage resources at local farms, mills, and mines.
- The mine is not clearable as none of the draugr are marked as the boss.
- Soljund's Sinkhole is the only settlement in the entire game (cut or otherwise) that does not get mentioned in the `CWScript`.

## Bugs

- The draugr respawn, making the quest repeatable and possibly killing the miners should you enter while they're at work.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
- The guard at the mine will always be an Empire-affiliated Reach Hold Guard, due to `SoljundSinkholeLocation` missing keywords for changing the garrison if the Stormcloaks take the Reach.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The guard at the mine may not respawn.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- Soljund's Sinkhole uses the wrong map icon. It is a mining settlement, but erroneously uses the [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") map icon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, addresses this issue. Soljund's Sinkhole now uses the map icon for [mines](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines").

Nelacar's staff

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any and all of the three following people. The quest item and its location is uniquely determined by the quest giver.

| Region | Location | Quest Giver | Quest Item | Target Location | Dialogue Trigger | Reward |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Argonian Assemblage](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Assemblage "Skyrim:Argonian Assemblage") | [Stands-In-Shallows](/wiki/Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows "Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows") | [Double-Distilled Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Distilled_Skooma "Skyrim:Double-Distilled Skooma") | [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") | "Are you all right?" | One Sneak skill point |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), [Dengeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Dengeir's House") | [Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") | [Private Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Letter "Skyrim:Private Letter") | [Lod's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod%27s_House "Skyrim:Lod's House") | "You say there's a plot against you?" | Leveled gold |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") | [Malur Seloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Malur_Seloth "Skyrim:Malur Seloth") | [Staff of Arcane Authority](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Arcane_Authority "Skyrim:Staff of Arcane Authority") | [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth") | "What do you do around here?" | One Speech skill point |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to the quest giver.
2. Steal the requested item.
3. Return to the quest giver.

### Dengeir of Stuhn

[Dengeir of Stuhn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dengeir_of_Stuhn "Skyrim:Dengeir of Stuhn") was once the Jarl of Falkreath but has since stepped down and is now a Thane. He is a paranoid and patriotic supporter of the Stormcloaks. He believes that [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") the blacksmith is writing a treasonous letter and wants you to steal it for him.

The letter is on Lod's bedside table. It is simply a note requesting extra iron. Steal it and return it to Dengeir. Dengeir will at first be confused, and then realize Lod is probably not up to treason, even if he is making extra weapons for the Empire. He will then give you a reward of leveled gold.

Completion of this quest opens up another radiant quest, [Dark Ancestor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Ancestor "Skyrim:Dark Ancestor").

### Malur Seloth

Talking to [Malur Seloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Malur_Seloth "Skyrim:Malur Seloth") and asking him what he does prompts him to reveal that he doesn't really do anything. He wants to appear more mage-like when in the jarl's presence, and wishes to acquire [a staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Arcane_Authority "Skyrim:Staff of Arcane Authority").

The one he wants belongs to [Nelacar](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelacar "Skyrim:Nelacar") who resides in the [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"). The staff is located in the shop counter in Nelacar's room. Steal it and return to Malur. He will reward you with one skill point in [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech").

### Stands-In-Shallows

When speaking to [Stands-In-Shallows](/wiki/Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows "Skyrim:Stands-In-Shallows"), he mentions that he overheard sailors talking about their stashed [extra powerful Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Distilled_Skooma "Skyrim:Double-Distilled Skooma"), and he would like to get it.

The bottle is located in the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") in Windhelm, underneath the second set of stairs. Steal it and return to Stands-in-Shallows, who will reward you with a skill point in [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak").

## Notes

- Only one radiant quest of a similar type can be assigned at any given time. You must clear the radiant quest from your miscellaneous quests in order to be eligible to receive another of the same type.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.
- This quest requires you to commit a [crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime"); see that page for details about criminal activity.
- Malur's and Shallows' items are available to retrieve from the start of the game, while the letter Dengeir requests only gets enabled once he has mentioned it.

## Bugs

- The quest might not trigger if you have already stolen the quest item before talking to the related NPC. Since the quest item is marked as such, you are left with no way of getting rid of it.

## Quest Stages

| Some Light Theft (Favor018) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Steal the <Alias=QuestItem> for <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Bring the <Alias=QuestItem> to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor018 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor018`.

# Skyrim:Sorli's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Sorli's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sorli%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| StonehillsSorlisHouse | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Sorli's House in Stonehills

**Sorli's House** is a one-room stone house and the home of [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder"), [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur"), and their son [Sirgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirgar "Skyrim:Sirgar").

It is the only house in [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur")  [Sirgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirgar "Skyrim:Sirgar")  [Sorli the Builder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") |

### Exterior

It is situated by [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") encampment and [Rockwallow mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine") which is run by [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur") and [Sorli](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") for [Thane Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), all the citizens of Stonehills including their son [Sirgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirgar "Skyrim:Sirgar") work in the iron ore mine. There is a small deck in front of the house with a wooden bench at one end and a pile of firewood at the other. There is an unusually high number of [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") and [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly "Skyrim:Butterfly") around the house and encampment.

### Sorli's House

Sorli's house

Inside it is a one room home. On your left upon entering is a cupboard holding nine [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot") and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). To the right is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel. Against the east wall is a long wooden table holding four pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and nine iron ingots, with two more on the floor under and beside the table. There is a second pickaxe leaning against the wall to the right of the table with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling above.

Against the south wall is another long wooden table and chair, this is where Sorli spends a lot of her time. On the table are two bottles of alto wine, a bottle of wine, several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), several pieces of cheese, a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") and a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). Above this table are three hanging racks holding four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). In the center of the south wall, opposite the door is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front. On the mantlepiece is a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")*.

To the right of the fireplace, coming out from the south wall is Sirgar's single unowned bed an to the right of this is a cupboard with three bunches of elves ear and two bunches of frost mirriam hanging from the ceiling above it. Coming out from the west wall is a large double bed where Sorli and Pactur sleep, there is an end table to the left holding a bottle alto wine and a bottle of wine. To the right of the bed is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Against the north wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot with a round table and chair beside this holding a bottle of wine, a loaf of bread and a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). There are four more pine thrush egg in a basket on the floor. Beside the table is a pile of firewood and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe").

## Notes

- If the Stormcloaks take over Hjaalmarch, they are all supposed to moved to [Highmoon Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Highmoon_Hall "Skyrim:Highmoon Hall"). Pactur is supposed to act as steward judging from his dialogue and faction. However, due to an oversight, Pactur stays in Stonehills. This is fixed by the Hearthfire add-on.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this house is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.

## Bugs

- Sirgar's bed is owned by StonehillsSorlisHouseFaction. Because of that, it is possible for either of his either parents to sleep in it, and for Sirgar to sleep in the double bed with the other parent. An example of this can be [seen here](https://i.ibb.co/K2pP8sn/Screen-Shot71.png).
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. Sirgar's bed is now specifically owned by him.

# Skyrim:Soul Cairn Horse Quest

## Overview
