[Arvak's Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Arvak's Skull")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. *(Optional)* Talk to a distraught [soul](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul#xx002b0d "Skyrim:Soul").
2. Find [Arvak's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Arvak's Skull").
3. Return to the soul.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest can only be started within the [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn"). It can be started one of two ways, either by interacting with the distraught [soul](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul#xx002b0d "Skyrim:Soul") or by simply finding [Arvak's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Arvak's Skull"). The soul who starts the quest can be found between where you enter and the large wall dividing the Soul Cairn. When first approaching him, you will hear him calling out to [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak") in distress, yelling, *"Arvak! Arvak, where are you? Arvak, please come back! Come back!"* and calling his name repeatedly. If you speak to him, he'll plead with you to help find Arvak. You'll have to ask him what he's talking about, and he'll explain, *"Arvak. My horse. We came to this horrible place together. We were attacked by monsters, so I told him to run."* He tells you how loyal Arvak is, and that the poor creature has been running for too long. He begs you to find Arvak's skull, giving you a quest to locate it. Arvak will then begin appearing at random and briefly running in the direction of his skull before disappearing again.

From the entrance to the Boneyard, where Valerica is, head directly east. You will be able to see the tower and the four ghosts surrounding it, kneeling as if in prayer. Upon approaching the skull, the souls will turn into [mistmen](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistman "Skyrim:Mistman"). After dealing with them, you are free to take the skull, causing the soul of its owner to materialize nearby, a short distance away from the shrine. He will thank you considerably, saying, *"He's such a loyal beast. Here, I'll teach you how to call him to you."* You will now have access to the spell [Summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak"), which allows you to summon Arvak both within and outside of the Soul Cairn. Arvak's behavior is similar to a regular [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"), though he will dissipate after 60 seconds from when you summon him if you are not mounted. As you walk away from the soul, he will express deep gratitude and joy to see his horse become free of that eternal prison; telling you, *"Goodbye, hero! Take good care of Arvak for me! Such a good horse."*

After you have spoken to [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak")'s rider, or if you decide simply to go to the skull initially and you are having trouble navigating the Cairn due to the poor in-game map visibility in comparison with the map presented below, try the following procedure:

Walk through the dividing wall between the two halves of the Cairn to the side containing the pentagonal building, and stand a point in front (the northernmost side) of the first *fully intact* gateway structure facing the southwestern barrier along the path. Check your map, and then use it
to rotate your character roughly 15 degrees East of North (to the right). Your gaze should be
fixed somewhere in between the southeastern most corner of the pentagonal building and the barrier
of the Cairn opposing it. Walk straight in that direction, taking care (using the compass
at the top of the screen) not to deviate from a straight path. The winding and discontinuous pathways beneath you are will only serve to get you lost, so *ignore them*. Travel in a straight line. If an obstacle comes in your way, or combat occurs and throws you off, re-orient yourself so that you are facing the same direction and are following the same line.
You will find the skull just past the point where your position relative to the southeastern
corner of the pentagon and the line you traversed is at a 90 degree angle. You will know that
you have found this point when you are able to turn back along the same line you came on (an about face, or 180 degree rotation, looking back in the same direction you came from),
then after turning 90 degrees to your right you will be directly facing the southeastern corner of the pentagonal building.
A short walk past this point traveling in the same direction will put you at [Arvak's Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Arvak's Skull"). When you reach the skull,
turn 15 degrees south of east and travel a hundred paces or so, then you will come across
[Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak")'s rider to conclude the quest.

## Map

Portal

Arvak's skull

")

Arvak's Rider (initial)

Arvak's Rider (after)

Arvak's skull and rider location

## Notes

- It is possible to complete the quest without killing the mistmen by sneaking and being undetected, taking Arvak's skull, and giving it to the soul. You can even be sneaking when speaking to the soul; the option will briefly appear as "pickpocket soul", but he will initiate dialogue with you regardless of you being completely hidden or not.

## Bugs

- Arvak's skull is not given to the soul upon completion and is kept.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- You may be unable to pick up Arvak's skull. **?**
  - Loading a previous save and then coming back seems to fix this.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC01SoulCairnHorseQuest2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC01SoulCairnHorseQuest2`.

| DLC01SoulCairnOrigin More Location Codes  DLC01SoulCairnBoneyardEntrance, DLC01SoulCairnCemetaryKeeper, DLC01SoulCairnCemetaryKeeper01, DLC01SoulCairnCemetaryKeeperStart, DLC01SoulCairnCraterKeeper, DLC01SoulCairnCraterKeeperStart, DLC01SoulCairnDragonLair, DLC01SoulCairnForestKeeper, SoulCairnHorseQuest, SoulCairnHorseQuest02, SoulCairnHuskMerchant, SoulCairnOffShoot, SoulCairnPOI01, SoulCairnPOI03, SoulCairnPOI04, SoulCairnPOI05, SoulCairnPOI06, SoulCairnPOI08, SoulCairnPOI09, SoulCairnPOIJiub, SoulCairnPOIMaze, SoulCairnPOIRJ02, SoulCairnPOIRJ05, SoulCairnPOIRJ06, SoulCairnPOIRJ07, SoulCairnPOIRJ08, SoulCairnPOIRJ09, SoulCairnPOIRJ10, SoulCairnStartAmbush, SoulCairnTest, SoulCairnTest2, SoulCairnTome01, SoulCairnTome02, SoulCairnTome03, SoulCairnWall01, SoulCairnWallPOI01 | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |

The Soul Cairn

The **Soul Cairn** is a [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion") haunted by lost [souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul "Skyrim:Soul").

Your first visit to the Soul Cairn will be with [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") during the *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* [main quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Quests#Main_Quests "Skyrim:Dawnguard Quests"). When Serana adds her blood to the other ingredients in the portal vessel in [Valerica's study](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Ruins#Valerica.27s_Study "Skyrim:Volkihar Ruins"), the stone circles on the lower level split open, rising up and spinning around to form a curved staircase leading down from the balcony to the portal. If you are not a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") or vampire lord, you will need to have part of your [soul trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)") by Serana. If you choose to have Serana soul trap you, Valerica will tell you to find the [soul essence gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Essence_Gem "Skyrim:Soul Essence Gem"). After you do, your soul trapped state will be undone, and all your stats will return to normal. Finding it before meeting her will also work.

The Soul Cairn is primarily inhabited by souls, wandering non-hostile spirits that were sent here because they were soul trapped before being killed. Interacting with these spirits, they will usually comment on how lost or confused they are or how desolate or horrible the Soul Cairn is. According to lore, when a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") is used, the soul it contained goes here.

For more information on the Soul Cairn, see [the lore article](/wiki/Lore:Soul_Cairn "Lore:Soul Cairn").

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub")**  **[Morven Stroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Morven_Stroud "Skyrim:Morven Stroud")**  **[Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul "Skyrim:Soul")**  **[Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica")** † | |

† She will relocate to her study once she is advised of [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon")'s death.

## Related Quests

- **[Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes")**: Explore [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar").
- **[Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death")**: Search for [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica") in the Soul Cairn.
- **[Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(quest) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (quest)")**: Learn a [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)").
- **[Impatience of a Saint](/wiki/Skyrim:Impatience_of_a_Saint "Skyrim:Impatience of a Saint")**: Collect the ten missing pages of [Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub")'s Opus.
- **[Soul Cairn Horse Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn_Horse_Quest "Skyrim:Soul Cairn Horse Quest")**: Find [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak")'s skull.

## Areas of Interest

- **[Boneyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneyard "Skyrim:Boneyard")** — An enclosed graveyard in the Soul Cairn.
- **[Reaper's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Reaper's Lair")** — An enclosed ruin in the Soul Cairn.

## Characteristics of the Soul Cairn

The portal that transported you to the Soul Cairn

The Soul Cairn is roughly shaped like a figure 8 when viewed from the entrance stairs. It is oriented with the stairs toward the southwest and the Boneyard entrance to the northeast. There are two massive walls in the Soul Cairn. One wall divides the figure 8 closer to the side with the entrance stairs, with one gap roughly in the center. The second wall surrounds the Boneyard, separating it from the Soul Cairn.

Once you arrive, you can see the stairs from the portal ascending to a hole in the sky surrounded by darkness. The sky within the Soul Cairn ranges in color from blue to black and purple. There are many black structures throughout this plane of Oblivion, including many seen beyond the boundary of the area, which is clearly defined as a shimmering blue magical barrier (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

The landscape is completely alien. Scattered throughout the Soul Cairn are black skeletal trees and bushes (with [soul husks](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Husk "Skyrim:Soul Husk") being the only plant in the plane that can be harvested), upright black stones similar to very large gravestones, and the bones and skulls of dragons. If you look straight up at the sky, you will see what appears to be a giant black hole.

There are many structures scattered throughout the Soul Cairn. Some of these are buildings containing a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), typically guarded by hostile creatures. The entrances to some of these structures are blocked by bars. Pairs of standing stones with glowing bluish-green balls near the top are located near these buildings. Hitting the orbs with ranged spells or bow shots will lower the bars, granting access to the interior.

A lightning attractor

You will also find well-like structures dotting the landscape. Most of these emit a purplish-white glow from the top, similar to the focus points in and around the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). Standing in these causes your health to regenerate. There are smaller wells that do not glow; jumping into these will teleport you to a nearby, previously inaccessible area.

Yet another type of structure you'll come across is the lightning attractor, which is activated by placing a [grand](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Grand Soul Gem") or [greater soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Greater Soul Gem") into a holder, which will then cause lightning to strike the rod, turning the [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") into an empty black soul gem. Using these lightning rods will summon several hostile creatures.

### Flora and Fauna

The flora here is unlike anything you've encountered in [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"). [Soul husks](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Husk "Skyrim:Soul Husk") are the strange clusters of sand-colored and sand-textured cones sticking up from the ground. They can be used to counter the effects of [Ideal Master Crystals](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Ideal_Master_Crystal "Skyrim:Traps"), the giant floating health-draining gems that may be found at the top of the various structures within the Soul Cairn. Soul husks are also the only currency used when trading with the spectral merchant, [Morven Stroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Morven_Stroud "Skyrim:Morven Stroud"), for various enchanted items and spell tomes.

Soul fissures are another common feature of the Soul Cairn; they are cracks in the ground with air rising visibly out of them, which causes them to emit a hissing noise. When you activate a soul fissure, it will fill the largest soul gem in your inventory, filling black soul gems first.

While traversing the Soul Cairn, you will be attacked by [bonemen](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneman "Skyrim:Boneman"), [wrathmen](/wiki/Skyrim:Wrathman "Skyrim:Wrathman"), and [mistmen](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistman "Skyrim:Mistman"). There are also a few unique creatures to be found here: the cursed dragon [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)"), three [keepers](/wiki/Skyrim:Keeper "Skyrim:Keeper") who maintain a barrier around the Boneyard, and the [Reaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper "Skyrim:Reaper").

Bonemen
:   Bonemen look like blue-black [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). Once defeated, they collapse like normal skeletons, but then their remains become soul embers, which are translucent black puddles similar in shape to a defeated [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith")'s remains. They typically carry [ancient Nord weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord#Draugr_Weapons "Skyrim:Ancient Nord"), which can be looted along with soul gems, various alchemical [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), [gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems "Skyrim:Gems"), [jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), and soul husks. They are the most common of the creatures found within the Soul Cairn.

Wrathmen
:   Wrathmen appear similar to ghostly [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), and typically carry random two-handed melee weapons. Their remains also turn to soul embers after dying. Their weapons, but not their armor, can be looted along with similar minor loot to bonemen.

Mistmen
:   Mistmen appear similar to the [corrupted shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Shade "Skyrim:Corrupted Shade") found in [Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins"), and seem to favor magic as their main form of attack, although they will pick up dropped weapons. Their remains also turn to soul embers after dying, and they carry similar minor loot to bonemen.

Keepers
:   The keepers are tall, armored foes with black, smoky heads, armed with [dragonbone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonbone "Skyrim:Dragonbone") weapons and carrying black soul gems. Their weapons, but not their armor, can be looted if your level is 45 or higher. When defeated, their bodies dissolve into *ghostly remains*, the same as the various [guardian spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Guardian_Spirit "Skyrim:Wolf Guardian Spirit") faced during [Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials").

## Walkthrough

#### Objective: Beyond Death:

The portal takes you to the southwestern edge of the Soul Cairn. There is a path heading north away from you. You can either choose to locate [Valerica](/wiki/Skyrim:Valerica "Skyrim:Valerica") immediately, by following the path in front of you to the entrance to the [Boneyard](#The_Boneyard), or explore the Soul Cairn first and locate Valerica once you have defeated the three keepers. The keepers are found by the tallest, most ornate towers in the Soul Cairn, and are siphoning power from lost souls to maintain the barrier surrounding the Boneyard. Once they have been defeated, the barrier surrounding the Boneyard will fall, enabling you to enter the Boneyard and obtain the [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Blood) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Blood)") located there.

### Southwest Corner of the Map: Near the Portal

There are several soul husks around the bottom of the stairs from the portal. By following the path north for a short distance, you will see a square black building on the right. There are stairs leading up to a doorway blocked by bars. To the left, on the ground, are a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). On either side of the doorway, you'll see standing stones with glowing orbs near the top. Shooting both of these with arrows or ranged spells will lower the bars, allowing you to access the interior. Inside is a chest containing a soul gem or two, while a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchantments "Skyrim:Enchantments") [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [page 8 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_8) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 8)"), and a random soul gem lie on the ground in front of it. A second soul gem is in a stand on the right.

Continuing along the road to the north, you will see another building a short way off to the right of the path. As you approach, you will be attacked by several bonemen, with some outside and others inside the building. There are open doorways to the interior on each side of the building, and several healing wells around the outside. Stepping into the small well just outside the building's northern entrance will teleport you to the roof of the building, where you will find a chest, with a copy of *[The Book of Life and Service](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Life_and_Service "Skyrim:The Book of Life and Service")* and a random soul gem in front of it. You may safely return to the ground by carefully jumping onto the lower roof of the structure from the southern corner of the roof. Inside the building, there is a chest in the western corner, with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a random soul gem, and [page 6 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_6) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 6)") on the ground in front of it.

[‡](#note_arv)**Objective: Arvak**

*Farther along the path, you will encounter a soul that appears to be looking for something or someone. When you approach, he will ask you to help find his horse, [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak"), starting a side quest to find [Arvak's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Arvak's Skull"). After this point, you may see Arvak, a skeletal horse with a blue flaming mane and tail. He will randomly teleport close to you, stand nearby, or gallop through the Soul Cairn. You are unable to interact with Arvak until you complete the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn_Horse_Quest "Skyrim:Soul Cairn Horse Quest") and learn the spell [Summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak").*

Continuing along the path, the path passes through a gap in a tall black stone wall, with a flight of stairs leading up to the gap.[‡](#intnote_arv) A healing well lies to the left, and beyond that to the west is a stone courtyard, with a building built into the wall. Inside the building is a chest containing quality loot. There is a wide exit on the far side of the room to the northwest. Upon exiting through that doorway, four bonemen will rise from the ground: two immediately in front of you, and two on another smaller structure ahead. Once they are dealt with, you can climb the stairs on the side of the structure ahead to find a chest filled with quality loot, with [page 3 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_3) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 3)") and a [copper and sapphire circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Copper_and_Sapphire_Circlet "Skyrim:Copper and Sapphire Circlet") on the ground in front of it. However, take care not to linger, as an Ideal Master Crystal hangs in the sky above the chest.

This structure is bisected by the barrier surrounding the Soul Cairn. There are two large healing wells beside the structure, but nothing else of interest is in the immediate area. Passing back through the building built into the wall, you have the choice of exploring the rest of this side of the great wall before passing through the gap, or heading straight for Valerica.

A scenic view of the Soul Cairn

Continuing your exploration, there is a path heading west. Following it will enable you to explore the left-hand side of the original path. There are several soul fissures for you to collect, as well as healing wells. When you arrive back at the stairs to the portal, you can cross and start exploring the other side, which is far larger.

There is a building east-southeast of the portal steps, with two random soul gems inside on the ground level on a stack of squared-off stones. A teleport well lies a few paces outside the building to the northeast. The well will transport you to the roof of the building, where you will be attacked by a boneman and a wrathman guarding a chest. You may safely return to ground level by jumping from the western corner of the roof.

Northwest of the teleport well, you'll see the spine of a dragon sticking out of the ground, with a human skull on top of it. In front of this gruesome totem stands a soul gem pedestal holding a black soul gem. Approaching will cause three bonemen to emerge from the ground and attack. A few steps south of the teleport well lie the skeletal remains of another dragon, with a human skeleton in its ribcage. There are [ancient Nord gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Gauntlets") and a [steel sword of shocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword_of_Shocks "Skyrim:Steel Sword of Shocks") inside the dragon's remains.

Near the southeastern corner of the Soul Cairn, a distance due east of the previous teleport well building, is a large structure with an interior courtyard where two soul husks grow. There is only one narrow doorway in or out, with several flights of stairs leading up from the courtyard to the top of the structure opposite a tower. If you are facing the tower, there are stairs on your left which descend to a lower roof. You can either use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") or descend the stairs, follow the roof along, and then climb another flight at the far end to reach the tower. At the top of the tower is an Ideal Master Crystal floating above another chest of quality loot.

A discernible path heading north from the doorway to the courtyard leads to a paved section with a lightning attractor beside a chest. Some skeletal remains and a soul gem are on the ground in front of the chest. Using the lightning attractor causes some bonemen and wrathmen to rise from bone piles around it.

### Middle of the Map: Between the Boneyard and the Portal

Morven Stroud is... er, was a Breton merchant

Head toward the gap in the great wall. A short distance before reaching it, there are stairs off to the east leading up to the rear of the wall, with a window that looks through to the other side. The window is flanked by flagpoles, and there is a soul standing beside it. Additionally, the stones at the base of the flagpoles hold [page 1 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_1) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 1)"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a copy of *The Book of Life and Service*, and a random filled soul gem. You can see a chest (which contains minor loot) through the window on the other side of the wall. To reach the chest, you need to pass through the gap in the wall and immediately turn east, then follow the wall until you reach a short flight of stairs leading up to the alcove containing the chest.

North of this chest, you will find [Morven Stroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Morven_Stroud "Skyrim:Morven Stroud"), a merchant from [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock") who wound up here after he double-crossed some [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"). He arrived with his horse and cart, and is the only merchant within the Soul Cairn. He is willing to trade 25 soul husks for any single random item. You can choose between a [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), a [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), a piece of [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor"), a piece of [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), or a spell tome. He has an unlimited supply of each option, so if you're after a specific enchantment, save and reload before speaking to him.

Morven can be found standing or sitting near his wagon; his skeleton is lying sprawled across the wagon seat, and can be freely looted for a few [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Some unusable barrels are at the wagon's rear, with [page 10 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_10) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 10)") sitting atop one of them.

A large building with a doorway blocked by bars lies immediately behind Morven. The orbs you need to shoot are on either side of you when facing the blocked doorway. The orb on the left is on top of the building. Inside the building, you'll find a chest containing minor loot. A few paces to the southwest of Morven Stroud is a flight of stairs leading up to a teleport well, which takes you to the pinnacle of the same building. Dropping from the northern corner leads to a flat section of roof, where you'll find another chest containing minor loot (you will only suffer minor damage from the fall).

#### The First Keeper and Conjure Wrathman Spell Tome

Following the main wall and barrier to the east leads to several structures. The first is a small many-arched structure containing nothing of interest. The second structure just beyond the first is a tall, ornate tower, with broken masonry spinning around its top, and what seems to be many souls congregating around a tall, armored figure at its base. This is one of the keepers. As you approach, up to four wrathmen will rise and attack. Once they are defeated, you will face the keeper, who carries a dragonbone battleaxe. During the fight, the souls that the keeper was draining will vanish.

Jiub wanders around his campsite

A few paces farther east lies another structure, with four pillars supporting it. Beneath the structure, you'll find a typical shrine base holding the *[Spell Tome: Conjure Wrathman](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Wrathman "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Wrathman")*. Upon approaching the spell tome, some wrathmen will attack. There is a path to the east of this structure; follow it to find the [Reaper's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Reaper's Lair"). On the east side of this building, you will find a skeleton leaning against a large rock, with a random enchanted [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") and an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet") lying beside it. There is also a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_(DG) "Skyrim:Note (DG)") next to the skeleton, which suggests this was an accomplished [adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer") who willingly entered the portal against someone's advice. More wrathmen will rise as you approach the skeleton.

#### Reaper's Lair and a Reaper Gem Fragment

The Reaper's Lair is the only building with a door within the Soul Cairn. To correctly call forth the reaper and its minions, you will normally need to collect three [reaper gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Reaper Gem Fragment"), although it is also possible to do this using [fire runes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Rune "Skyrim:Fire Rune") (see [notes](#Notes)). Full details for the lair are found [on the relevant page](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaper%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Reaper's Lair").

Heading north from the Reaper's Lair, you'll come to a large paved area with several structures and flights of stairs that lead up to a lightning attractor. Using it will cause some bonemen, wrathmen, and mistmen to attack. Head southwest, passing the spiked roof of a building, to another paved area with a well in the middle. As you approach, bonemen will attack you. Beside the well is a skull, a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), a random enchanted [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), [page 5 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_5) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 5)"), a random poison, and three empty random soul gems.

#### Objective: Impatience of a Saint:

North of the well, you will encounter [Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub") sitting beside or walking around an extinguished campfire while muttering to himself. He was a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") adventurer from [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and was killed by [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") in [Kvatch](/wiki/Lore:Kvatch "Lore:Kvatch") during the [Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion_Crisis "Lore:Oblivion Crisis"). You can speak to him to learn more about him, and offer your services to help him find ten pages of his notes so he may write the second volume of his autobiography. This will initiate the quest [Impatience of a Saint](/wiki/Skyrim:Impatience_of_a_Saint "Skyrim:Impatience of a Saint"). Once you've collected all ten pages of his book, you will be able to see the details in Jiub's form far more clearly. He will be overjoyed, and will reward you with a unique book, *[Saint Jiub's Opus](/wiki/Skyrim:Saint_Jiub%27s_Opus "Skyrim:Saint Jiub's Opus")*, as well as the [locket of Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Locket_of_Saint_Jiub "Skyrim:Locket of Saint Jiub").

[†](#note_qc)**Objective: Arvak**

*Northeast of this complex is an open-sided tower with a shrine base in the middle underneath; Arvak's skull is on top of it. As you approach, you will be attacked by several bonemen and mistmen. Once you have dealt with them, take the skull. Arvak's owner, whom you spoke with earlier, will appear a short walk east of your location, beside a healing well. He will teach you a spell to summon Arvak when you speak with him.*

To the west is a large structure, with a path leading around behind a wall. As you approach, several bonemen, wrathmen, and mistmen will all attack. A well is in the northern corner of the structure. Nearby, along the northeast wall, a random enchanted [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe") is on the same raised section of paved ground as the well.

Arvak's deceased owner is overjoyed that his horse is safe

The entrance to yet another structure is nearby to the southwest.[†](#intnote_qc) Enter the structure and look to your right for a teleport well that takes you to the roof. There is an Ideal Master Crystal hanging above a chest, which contains one of the reaper gem fragments in addition to quality loot. There is a second, lower level to the southwest, featuring at the far southwest end another chest of minor loot with a sack of soul husks beside it.

#### Conjure Mistman Spell Tome

From the location of Arvak's skull, continue northeast to find another tower with a teleport well inside. As you approach, some bonemen, wrathmen, and mistmen will attack you from the roof as well as from the ground. You can teleport directly to the roof and then fight your way back down. Two flights of stairs down from the top, on the first covered section, is a copy of *The Book of Life and Service*. On the next level down, you can see part of a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"); casting any magic at it will cause another boneman to rise.

The Conjure Mistman spell tome rests upon its plinth

Back on ground level, another dragon carcass with an enchanted battleaxe and a few orcish arrows lies a couple feet north of the stairs. A few paces farther to the east lies a staircase leading up to a paved section, where you'll find a plinth holding the *[Spell Tome: Conjure Mistman](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Mistman "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Mistman")*. There is a medium coin purse, an empty random soul gem, and [page 7 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_7) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 7)") on the ground at the base of the shrine. You will summon several angry mistmen upon approaching the spell tome.

#### The Second Keeper and a Reaper Gem Fragment

North-northwest of the shrine is a teleport well with three pillars around it and two healing wells beside it, all underneath a floating island. Entering the teleport well transports you to a structure on top of the island. Following the path around the structure counter-clockwise as you climb, you will pass several souls before reaching a keeper armed with a dragonbone bow. Behind the keeper is another teleport well, which returns you to the ground beside the first well. Head west, and you will soon see another large building with an Ideal Master Crystal floating above it. Inside, a staircase leads all the way to the roof, where a chest containing quality loot (including one of the reaper gem fragments) and a copy of *The Book of Life and Service* are sitting directly under the crystal.

Heading southwest, up the hill toward the Boneyard, you will see a building situated against the eastern wall, with several flights of stairs leading up to it. At the top of the first flight of stairs, you will see a short, covered passage on your right. There is a chest at the end of the passage, with [page 4 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_4) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 4)") and two pieces of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") sitting on the ground beside it. As you approach the chest, a mistman will rise from the nearby pile of bones.

A path heading south from this building leads to a healing well surrounded by upright stones. Turning and heading southwest leads past a soul acting as a farmer. The soul is tilling the land where fourteen soul husks are planted, as two [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") souls wander freely nearby.

#### Conjure Boneman Spell Tome

Head west from the large complex west of Jiub's camp to find a large raised paved area with stairs leading up to a lightning attractor. Using the attractor will cause some bonemen, wrathmen, and mistmen to rise and attack. From here, head north-northwest through a fairly barren area, and you'll eventually reach a large structure, with two tall pillars of black stonework that mark the beginning of an underpass. The path begins on the southern side of the structure, with several bonemen patrolling the underpass. Inside the building, stairs lead up and counter-clockwise until you reach an Ideal Master Crystal hanging inside the building above a chest containing quality loot.

To the southwest is a paved area where a soul is standing over a lootable skeleton with a large coin purse beside it. There is a building nearby, with stairs leading up to a barred area and an Ideal Master Crystal hanging in the sky above. As you reach the top, several bonemen will rise. One of the orbs that you need to hit to lower the bars is above them; the other is under the pitched roof farthest from the bars, somewhat hidden behind some stacked stone slabs. A chest containing quality loot with a soul sitting beside it lies beyond the barred gate.

To the west, you'll find a plinth sitting on some stonework surrounded by several soul husks. Beside the plinth lies the *[Spell Tome: Conjure Boneman](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Boneman "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Boneman")*, two random soul gems, and a sack of soul husks. As you approach, a horde of at least five bonemen will assault you.

#### The Third Keeper and a Reaper Gem Fragment

Farther to the west is another large building, the Tabernacle of the Ideal Masters. As you near it, you will pass under a small arch and ascend a short flight of stairs. On the far side are several bonemen, wrathmen, and mistmen. A keeper is leaning against the wall in front of you, armed with a dragonbone mace.

To the left lies another short flight of stairs leading up to an area blocked by a gate. One of the control orbs is on your right at eye level, and the other is high above the blocked doorway. Shoot these to access an area with another Ideal Master Crystal floating over a chest containing one of the reaper gem fragments and some quality loot. As you approach the chest, some bonemen will attack. Take care, as you may be within range of the Ideal Master Crystal during the fight.

There is a teleport well to the right of the keeper through the arch opposite the barred gate, which takes you to the top of an L-shaped roof section above the well. There is a quality chest at the other end of the roof, and a lightning attractor where the roof turns. Using this will cause some bonemen and wrathmen to rise from the piles of bones on either side of the attractor.

North of the main structure, you'll find a teleport well in a small paved area with many upright stones around it. The well takes you to a raised platform, where a mistman attacks you near a dead traveler's camp. Here, a skeleton lies near an extinguished campfire. Near the campfire, you will find three random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a random potion or poison, a [scroll of storm thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Storm_Thrall "Skyrim:Scroll of Storm Thrall"), a [dragon priest dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Dagger "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Dagger"), a random [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff "Skyrim:Staff"), a large coin purse, three soul husks, and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"). Take care when dropping back down to the ground, or use the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout to avoid damage.

An alchemy lab located to the left of the Boneyard's entrance

East-northeast of the building containing the keeper is a large, complex structure, the Black Minster. The main entrance is on the southern side, which leads into a maze of short dead-end passages where an occasional boneman, wrathman, or mistman guard two chests. There is a sack of soul husks in the corridor near one of the chests, which also has a copy of *The Book of Life and Service* beside it on the ground. There are two loose soul husks and a [daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on a platform to your left near the passage with horizontal bars at either end.

#### The Soul Essence Gem

The passages eventually lead to a teleport well with grating above it, which takes you directly above. Stairs lead up to a chest under an Ideal Master Crystal. The chest will be empty if you're a vampire, but will contain the soul essence gem if you had Serana trap part of your soul. Around the far side of the chest is [page 9 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_9) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 9)") and a random empty soul gem.

On the west side of the entrance to the Boneyard is a large structure with an inner courtyard, the Black Folly, accessed by a narrow passage. Inside you will find what looks like a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), in front of which lies a typical boss chest, [page 2 of *Jiub's Opus*](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub%27s_Opus_(Page_2) "Skyrim:Jiub's Opus (Page 2)"), a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), and a small coin purse. Return to Jiub to complete his quest, then head to the entrance of the Boneyard.

Approaching the entrance to the Boneyard, you will find Valerica, who rushes to her daughter. She has set up an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") to the left of the Boneyard's entrance, and several books can be found nearby: *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*, *[Physicalities of Werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Physicalities_of_Werewolves "Skyrim:Physicalities of Werewolves")*, and *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*. Three rolls of paper and three soul husks are also beside the alchemy lab. After a conversation between you and Valerica, she will lead the way into the Boneyard.

#### The Boneyard

The [Boneyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Boneyard "Skyrim:Boneyard") is an enclosed graveyard within the Soul Cairn that is only accessible after defeating the three keepers. Upon entering the Boneyard, you will pass along a narrow passage before it opens into a large courtyard. Surrounding the central courtyard are raised sections, with stairs leading up to healing wells. As soon as you enter, Durnehviir will be flying around in the sky, and bonemen will begin to rise. It is best to concentrate on fighting the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragons "Skyrim:Dragons"), as bonemen will continue to rise to replace their fallen until you defeat Durnehviir, at which point any remaining bonemen will immediately die.

## Notes

- Serana is the only follower who can enter the Soul Cairn with you. However, anyone you resurrect outside the Soul Cairn, such as via the [Ritual Stone's](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") power, will follow you in.
- An easy way to navigate the Soul Cairn is to follow the edges; don't stray too far from them. Almost all locations here are near the edges of the playable area, or within sight of one.
- You won't be allowed entry into the Soul Cairn unless you either are a vampire, or let Serana partially soul trap you. If you let yourself be partially soul trapped, you'll get the [Weakened Soul](/wiki/Skyrim:Weakened_Soul "Skyrim:Weakened Soul") ability; your magicka, health, and stamina will be reduced by 45 points and recover slowly. You can reverse it if you pick up the [Soul Essence Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Essence_Gem "Skyrim:Soul Essence Gem"); all 3 stats will be restored, and recover normally.
- You can quickly return to the Soul Cairn without having to traverse the [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") ruins and courtyard again by exiting the laboratory through a door in the southern corner. This leads to the *Castle Volkihar Balcony*, a small outside area from which you can fast-travel and then return to the Soul Cairn via the door to the laboratory.
- If you view the map while in the Soul Cairn, the marker will place you in the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"), just north of [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear").
- All enemies defeated here, except for Durnehviir, will have at least one soul gem in their inventory.
- The bonemen, mistmen, and wrathmen may have soul husks in their inventories, and some of them may also drop [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), making them the only respawning enemies in the game that drop ectoplasm.
- Once the enemies here are defeated, they cannot be resurrected in any way.
- Soul husks in your inventory are classified as food, not ingredients.
- If the [Green Thumb](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Thumb "Skyrim:Green Thumb") perk is active, you will gain 2 soul husks per harvest, rather than one.
- There aren't many animal and creature souls present here, despite it being the place where spent souls go to after being used in soul gems. This could prove Serana's theory that only the souls used in black soul gems end up in the Soul Cairn. However, 2 cow souls can be found in a pseudo farm setting, and Arvak himself can be seen roaming around. There is no explanation for their presence.
- Other than the human-shaped souls you'll find here, there is another entity that roams the Soul Cairn. They look and behave like recolored [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp"), though they are completely docile and you cannot interact with them in any way. However, if you attract the attention of hostile enemies and then evade detection, they will target the wisp-like entities instead. This can be a useful distraction since the wisp-like entities are invulnerable, and the undead don't seem to realize that.
- The rods for the lightning attractors will eventually reset, though the attractors themselves can only be used once. The soul fissures aren't restricted to one-time use, though, allowing you to reactivate them when the Soul Cairn resets.
- A half-buried word wall exists here, though it isn't active.
- Several [Daedra Hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") can be found here, making it an alternative way to get them for free.
- As the Soul Cairn is technically outside, it is possible to use the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") shout to summon a storm. The area becomes cloudy, and almost appears as if it's part of Tamriel. You cannot fast travel from here, though.
- According to lore, after a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") is used, the soul it contained goes here. However, in-game this doesn't happen, and the soul is simply used and the gem disappears.
- [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star"), the [Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star_(item) "Skyrim:The Black Star (item)"), the [Flawed Varla Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawed_Varla_Stone "Skyrim:Flawed Varla Stone")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Curios "Skyrim:Rare Curios"), and the [Soul Tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Tomato "Skyrim:Soul Tomato")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_and_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints and Seducers") won't be filled if you activate a soul fissure here.
- One of the Keepers uses a bow with dragon bone arrows that may not be retrieved based on your character level, but can be task retrieved by Serana. You will need to hold the speech action button with the cursor pointed on the floor in front of her feet to enable command actions for her.
- When [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") is active, you will be unable to dismiss Serana from your party while the two of you are here.
- Serana's "I need you to do something" dialogue option will be absent while the two of you are here. However, if you hold down the speech action key while pointing the cursor in front of her, she will then be able to perform actions upon your request like other followers. Don't tell Serana to "wait" while you're here, though, or she'll get bugged.

## Bugs

- In the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition"), you may experience significantly reduced framerates while in the Soul Cairn.
  -  Use the console command `tg` to completely disable grass display while in the Soul Cairn. (Repeat the command to reenable grass, if desired.) You may have to do this multiple times as you explore.
- Killing the enemies in the Soul Cairn might freeze the game if their remains fall between rocks or partially sink below the ground. **?**
- The Soul Cairn may be reentered at any time. However, if you first enter as a vampire and are subsequently cured of vampirism, you'll need to become a vampire again in order to reenter.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.8, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=26730)) It enables you to reenter even as a mortal, since Valerica's dialogue implies this to be possible.
  - If you turn back into a vampire in Valerica's study, you'll need to exit and reenter the room before you'll be able to reenter the Soul Cairn.
  - The Special Edition for Xbox appears to have this bug already fixed.
- Sometimes after defeating Durnehviir, Valerica will tell you to follow her, but will then not move.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=32525))
  - Using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout will blow her away, after which she may pick herself up and begin moving normally again. However, this may not always work.
- It is possible to pass beyond the blue barrier surrounding the Soul Cairn. In the first half of the world, access an enclosed area (where page 3 of *Jiub's Opus* can be found) through a building to the left of the passage to the other half. There is an invisible gap between the wall to the left and the barrier through which you may pass.
- The "health drain" visual effect may remain on your character, even when you are not in range of one of the Ideal Master Crystals. The health drain effect does not follow, but the visual effect can become obstructive. This is easily remedied by walking within range of one of the crystals without using the effects of a soul husk, and then stepping away.
- The Conjure Mistman spell tome may be stuck at the bottom of the podium with only one corner visible, and not able to be grabbed.
  -  A workaround is to press ~ to bring up the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), enter `tcl` to enable noclip mode, and go underneath the pedestal to reach the tome. Then, return above ground and enter `tcl` to disable noclip mode again.
  - You can also shoot an arrow at the tome to knock it down.
- Mannequins may be randomly seen on the stairs, blocking doorways, or floating around, but if you save and reload or point the camera away from them, they will disappear. **?**
- Using [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") here will light up the Soul Cairn, and can cause it to stay lit even after the Shout's duration is complete. **?**
- Summoning [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)") here may cause him to end up running the same dialogue as though you had summoned him in Tamriel.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.1.4, fixes this bug.
- You may be able to successfully use [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") here. This doesn't make sense, since the Soul Cairn is a plane of Oblivion and thus never experiences normal Tamrielic weather.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.0, fixes this bug.
- At night, you might see [Masser](/wiki/Lore:Masser "Lore:Masser") and [Secunda](/wiki/Lore:Secunda "Lore:Secunda") in the sky, even though you are obviously not in Tamriel.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18321))
- Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch") can cause the glowing light orbs you have to hit to open gates in the Soul Cairn to turn invisible.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- Summoning [Fire Wyrms](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Wyrm "Skyrim:Fire Wyrm")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") here via your [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") shout with the [Dragonborn Flame](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Flame "Skyrim:Dragonborn Flame")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") ability active can cause the Fire Wyrms to be hostile towards the lost souls.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. Both factions have been set as allies to each other.
- The entry way from the Soul Cairn into the Boneyard may lack finalization on the navmesh under the door which can result in NPCs being unable to follow you in.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, fixes this bug.
- Parts of the mausoleum may not cast shadows even though they're solid stone chunks and the chunks themselves are easily visible.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- Running around here with a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") equipped can occasionally cause it to get stuck and not fire, making it impossible for you to run, jump, or shoot. **?**
  - Draw and/or sheath your crossbow, or open the character menu. Your crossbow should now function like normal.
- When using [Dawnbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnbreaker "Skyrim:Dawnbreaker") within the Soul Cairn, the mass turning effect from exploding undead can sometimes cause neutral souls to enter combat. While they will not attack and cannot be harmed, Serana will become stuck constantly casting spells at them until you load a previous save or fast travel. **?**
- The sky may be corrupted once you exit the Reaper's Lair.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130, fixes this bug.
- The skeleton by the Reaper's Lair is not detected by the [Detect Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Dead "Skyrim:Detect Dead") spell. **?**

Southfringe Sanctum

**Southfringe Sanctum** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing the conjurer [Bashnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Bashnag "Skyrim:Bashnag") and his [coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)"). It contains only one zone, *[Southfringe Sanctum](#Southfringe_Sanctum)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Savior of Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri")**: Help a necromancer escape from Southfringe Sanctum.
- **[The Rising Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rising_Dead "Skyrim:The Rising Dead")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead"): A group of [Necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") plan to summon an army of [zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Zombie "Skyrim:Zombie").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The entrance is marked by a lit brazier on a stand to the right. To the left is a table with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a set of [robes of quickening](/wiki/Skyrim:Robes_of_Quickening "Skyrim:Robes of Quickening") on top. There is a [spellsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)") working at the lab, who may be so absorbed in their work, they may be easy to sneak up upon. Prior to entering, to the north of the cave is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") beneath a rock overhang. Continuing to the north, by the base of a tree on the cliffs where one can overlook [Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad"), a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") you can't interact with and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") are found. In front of the chest is the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Warrior's Charge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrior%27s_Charge "Skyrim:The Warrior's Charge")*, and on the skeleton is an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). Due west, uphill behind a large rock outcrop, is a second silver ore vein. Due south of the cave entrance, along the path to the blocked gate leading to [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil"), lies a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"). Two more moonstone ore veins can be found 510 feet southwest of the cave entrance.

### Southfringe Sanctum

Southfringe Sanctum interior

The entrance leads into a natural passage heading west. There is a lantern on the ground shortly after entering the cave; just after this lantern, behind a plant on the other side of the tunnel, there is an unlocked chest. There is a spellsword patrolling this part of the tunnel. After a few paces, you come to a pair of wooden gates in a wider passage. Use caution, as the gates have a [frost rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Rune "Skyrim:Frost Rune") on them. Through the gates is a huge chamber filled with trees and vegetation on multiple levels. There is a spellsword standing on a ledge to the west of the gates. From the gates, two paths lead deeper into the cave system: a path heading west, beneath the spellsword, and another rising to the northwest. This second path ultimately leads to Bashnag, the leader of this spellsword coven, while the former path leads down to a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider")'s lair, through a system of caves infested with more [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").

Following the higher of the paths leads past two lit braziers on the ground on your right. Just past the second brazier, there's a flag on the left, by a mammoth rib cage. Turning south here then continuing forward leads to a unique [fox](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox "Skyrim:Fox") named [Pumpkin](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumpkin "Skyrim:Pumpkin"). Unfortunately, the cute little fox is hostile, and has likely eaten his last [chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") as you pass through the room. There is a small novice-locked cage containing a dead chicken behind Pumpkin, with two raw [chicken breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Chicken Breast") beside the cage. Beyond this is a spellsword who is either working at an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") or mining an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Beside the anvil is a table holding a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a piece of [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore"), a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"), a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons") [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). There is also a small empty tent nearby. A short distance north of the iron ore vein is a silver ore vein, and by a tree in front of this is a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), with a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") by a large tree stump farther north.

Returning to the main path and continuing to follow it as it rises, you will encounter another spellsword working at another alchemy lab. By this lab the path turns to the west, before ending at a pair of wooden gates. The gates are novice-locked, and open to reveal a path descending into an open-roofed chamber. You will find Bashnag working at an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") at the end. He, like all the other diligent workers in this cave, may hardly seem to notice you. He carries a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[The Art of War Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Art_of_War_Magic "Skyrim:The Art of War Magic")*. There is an unlocked boss chest to the right. A short distance before the enchanter, on the left and heading south, is a path that descends; to the right of the path is a small crevice in the rock wall with a lit brazier behind it. You can look through this and spy a spellsword in the room beyond. There is a second spellsword farther back, which enables you to take them out individually. The second spellsword is guarding a pair of unlocked wooden gates that block access to the beginning of the frostbite spiders' lair.

Past the gates, there are two spiders in the immediate vicinity, and an earthen bridge spanning the chamber; from this bridge you can reach a ramp leading up to two [egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac") that can be harvested. Beneath these is the passage that leads farther into the lair, and another short passage that leads to an area where you'll encounter [Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:Selveni Nethri") caught in webbing. She's a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") who was originally part of Bashnag's coven, but after a falling out, was chased and trapped down here. This was after Bashnag cursed her, making it impossible for her to cast any spells. She asks for your assistance in helping her escape, but will only leave once you've cleared the way. There are two more egg sacs in this lower passage, one of them behind Selveni. Use caution, as there are numerous spiders in this part of the cave system. As you pass through into the next chamber, which is circular, a giant frostbite spider will descend from above. The path follows the outer wall counterclockwise around the room and descends, passing an unlocked chest wedged behind a pillar on the left near the bottom. Just after the lowest point, there is another egg sac stuck to the ceiling that you can harvest. From this point, the passage rises steeply, before several turns lead back to the start of the two paths near the cave entrance. Once the caves are completely cleared, you can return and tell Selveni the coast is clear. There is no reward for completing this [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri").

## Notes

- The cave appears to be very buggy, with odd item placement and enemy behavior.
- A necromantic ritual site can be found north of the cave's entrance if the [Plague of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Plague_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Plague of the Dead") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed. See the [quest page](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rising_Dead "Skyrim:The Rising Dead") for more information.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- Selveni may not leave the cavern, leaving the quest unfinished. This can be fixed by commanding a follower to attack her, which will push her through the exit and complete the quest. Using various shouts such as Ice Form and Unrelenting Force on her may also work, as well as using archery. Alternatively, when she pauses at the exit, simply leaving the cavern and then immediately reentering may update and complete the quest.
- Behind the chest near Bashnag is a small, but accessible, hole in the wall that leads to the void outside the level. To get back, just walk through any wall (they are all one-way).
- It's possible to explore the areas above Bashnag's room and enter the void part of the level or get stuck.
- Sometimes it is not possible to enter the cave. You will move into the zone where the game should start loading the inside of the cave, but nothing happens, and no "To Southfringe Sanctum" label appears. **?**
  -  To fix this, exit the game (with command `qqq`) and start it again, loading from where you are just in front of the cave. The cave should be accessible now. If the same happens when attempting to exit the cave, just use `coc SouthfringeSanctumExterior`.
- Humanoid NPCs that are working will be non-hostile and will only become hostile once interacted with, making them easy prey for sneak attacks and [pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket").
- Although intended to be hostile to you, it is possible for Pumpkin the fox to spawn in a calm state. This may also be related to the fox spawning outside of its cage rather than being trapped within it.
- Pumpkin may also spawn in a hostile state but then become non-hostile when the spellswords are slain, provided he is not attacked in the process. **?**

# Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Worldspace: Sovngarde  ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Sovngarde "Lore:Sovngarde")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"), [Tsun](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsun "Skyrim:Tsun") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| SovngardeAlduinPerch, SovngardeCenter, SovngardeMeadHall, SovngardeNorth, SovngardeStart | |

Sovngarde

**Sovngarde** is the [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") afterlife.

The ruined word wall in Sovngarde

It is the realm of [Aetherius](/wiki/Lore:Aetherius "Lore:Aetherius") where dead Nord heroes are rewarded by [Shor](/wiki/Lore:Shor "Lore:Shor") with an eternity of revelry in the [Hall of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Valor "Skyrim:Hall of Valor"). It is here where you must defeat [Alduin the World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

## Residents

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | [Hall of Valor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Valor "Skyrim:Hall of Valor") | | --- | | **[Erlendr](/wiki/Skyrim:Erlendr "Skyrim:Erlendr")**  **[Felldir the Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Felldir_the_Old "Skyrim:Felldir the Old")**  **[Gormlaith Golden-Hilt](/wiki/Skyrim:Gormlaith_Golden-Hilt "Skyrim:Gormlaith Golden-Hilt")**  **[Hakon One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Hakon_One-Eye "Skyrim:Hakon One-Eye")**  **[Hunroor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunroor "Skyrim:Hunroor")**  **[Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:Jurgen Windcaller")**  **[Nikulas](/wiki/Skyrim:Nikulas "Skyrim:Nikulas")**  **[Olaf One-Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye")**  **[Ulfgar the Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfgar_the_Unending "Skyrim:Ulfgar the Unending")**  **[Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor "Skyrim:Ysgramor")** | | | Sovngarde (place) | | --- | | **[Froki Whetted-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki_Whetted-Blade "Skyrim:Froki Whetted-Blade")** ‡ **[Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist")** † **[High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg")**  **[Imperial Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier")**  **[Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")** \* **[Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke")** † **[Stormcloak Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier_(Sovngarde) "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier (Sovngarde)")**  **[Svaknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Svaknir "Skyrim:Svaknir")** § **[Tsun](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsun "Skyrim:Tsun")**  **[Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")** † | |

† Depends on how far you have advanced through the Skyrim [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), and the side that you have chosen.
‡ Depends on if he is killed during the game.
§ Depends on the completion of the quest [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames").

## Related Quests

- **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)")**: Seek out [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") within Sovngarde.
- **[Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer")**: Put an end to the [World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin").

### Sovngarde

Despite it being a place for the dead, the living may visit Sovngarde, provided they have a way to get there. Your only means of accessing Sovngarde is the portal created by the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Nahkriin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(creature) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (creature)") atop [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn") during the quest [The World-Eater's Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:The_World-Eater%27s_Eyrie "Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie"). You will find much of the land is shrouded in fog, with Alduin flying the skies, swooping down and devouring the very souls of his hapless victims.

The land itself is rich and vibrant, with flora and fungi including [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") plants, and the occasional patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") on tree stumps. There are no creatures in Sovngarde. Large identical statues line the stairs and the edges of the valley. Atop the central hill are the remains of a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), now covered in large rocks. The most notable feature of Sovngarde is the Hall of Valor, also known as Shor's Hall, a massive stone mead hall where dead Nord heroes are rewarded by Shor with an eternity of revelry.

During the quest [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)"), the Skuldafn portal brings you to the head of the valley at the top of a series of stairs. To reach the Hall of Valor, simply descend the stairs and follow the partly paved path that winds through the valley to the gatekeeper, [Tsun](/wiki/Skyrim:Tsun "Skyrim:Tsun"). On the way, you are likely to encounter several souls lost in the fog, mostly those of unnamed [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") or [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier"), but also the souls of certain named Nords who have died bravely. Most of the souls present will vary depending on your progress and choices in certain quests. However, [High King Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg") can always be found in the fog.

The Hall of Valor is on a pinnacle of rock separated from the rest of Sovngarde by a massive chasm spanned by a whalebone bridge. Tsun stands in front of the bridge between two stream-fed pools that empty over the edge of the chasm as great waterfalls. When you reach Tsun, he will ask by what right you should be allowed to enter the hall. Depending on your progress in various questlines, you may have several responses to choose from. Whichever right you claim, you must then prove your worth in a warrior's duel. Once you reduce Tsun's health sufficiently, the fight will stop, and you will be allowed to proceed across the bridge. On the far side, a paved terrace features two curved flights of stairs ascending to a row of four doors that all lead into the hall.

## Notes

- Although Sovngarde will technically respawn after ten days, there is no way to return to it after the main quest without the use of console commands. It is one of the few places in the game that cannot be revisited, so be sure not to leave anything behind.
- If you attempt to cross the bridge to the hall without dueling Tsun, you will be killed by lightning strikes on the bridge, even in [god mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"). You will also automatically die if you fall into the chasm beneath the bridge, though not in god mode.
- It is possible to kill and soul trap the generic soldiers and Svaknir. Their bodies will be removed after Alduin appears.
- Even though they're technically dead, the [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") spell, and not the [Detect Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Dead "Skyrim:Detect Dead") spell, will detect the heroes of Sovngarde.
- Sovngarde is said to be ruled by Shor, but he does not appear in the game.
- The "stars" slowly move across the sky of Sovngarde.
- The [constellations](/wiki/Lore:Constellations "Lore:Constellations") of [the Warrior](/wiki/Lore:The_Warrior_(constellation) "Lore:The Warrior (constellation)"), [the Thief](/wiki/Lore:The_Thief "Lore:The Thief"), and [the Mage](/wiki/Lore:The_Mage "Lore:The Mage") can be seen in the sky of Sovngarde.
- The chasm that spans the waterfalls next to the whalebone bridge has water at the bottom. This can be seen if you have the Eagle Eye perk in the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill tree when standing either on the bridge or on the rock outcroppings near the waterfalls.
- When you're not looking at them, the towering statues of the hooded figures turn to face you as you travel around Sovngarde. This is most notably seen when you walk down the stairs after entering from Skuldafn: if you turn back around, the statues that had been facing the stairs will have turned to face you at the bottom of the steps.

## Bugs

- Alduin's death cry during [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer") may be too quiet for you to hear if you're too far away.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
